halowed pthe day sonday hath ben ordeyned mynde recreacyon creature resonable maad resurrexyon ihesu cryst whyche aroos suche day semblably frestys sayntes solempnytees commauded chyrche kepte also erthely corporelle except foure caases fyrst haue necessyte lyf second necessyte lyf neyghbour thyrd necessyte holy chyrche fourth thauctoryte souerayn comandement whan suche dayes comandeth werke ony cause iuste resonable whiche foure caases leefful creature sayd dayes werke corporelle pthe second thynge wherof thumayn creature ought cesse especyal sayd dayes synne especyal dedely synne wel creature ought kepe hym self synne especyal dedely neuertheles synne doon sayd dayes moche greuous dayes third thynge wherof creature ought kepe hym sayd dayes ydlenes ydle cause ouer moche euyl synnes especyal sayd dayes ought creature occupye enbesye hym thre thynges fyrst makyng sacrefyse god hym self al hath especyal creature ought sayd dayes gyue hym selfe god deuoute orysons prayer haue grete sorow bytter repetauce hys synnes secondly creature ouzt occupye hym loange praysyng maker creatour cause mouthe synner preysyng playsaunt god euery creature ought make clene herte fro al synnes bytter repentaunce deuoute confessyon penaunce pthyrdly creature ought occupye hym sayd dayes doyng almesses loue god suche goodes god hath gyuen hym haue nede necessyte largely ought gyuen sayd dayes also yet dayes festys sayntes creature ought torne hys entendement consyderacyon thre thynges p fyrst creature ought consyder grete lyberalyte largesse god saynt whome feste lytyl seruyce hath doen god god hath gretely rewarded guerdoned hath gyuen hym glorye ioye pardurable wyth hym wyth god wyl creature honoured preysyd world consyderacion creature ought al toward god ouzt desyre wyth al herte doubte loue serue deuoutelye perseuerantly suche lord payeth wel hys seruauntes psecondly creature ought herte ymagyne thynke glorye ioye saynt hath wyth god whiche grete herte humayn may thynke ne mowthe expresse ne speke suche consyderacyon desyre haue suche wele creature desyre wyth al herte serue loue drede god whiche gyueth suche wele creature pthyrdly creature ought consyder sayd dayes grete myserye hym self dyuers trybulacyons afflyctyons maladyes euyl accydentes fortune seruytudes many moo parylles ben euery day thys poure world consyderacon creature ought haue world despyte preyse worldly thynges serue god al power desyre oute myserye haue grete ioye glorye heuen saynt hath wyth god phere folowen seuen comandementes apparteynyng loue dylection neyghbour capo x thre comandementes aforesayd apparteynyng loue dylectyon god folowe seuen apparteynyng loue neyghbour accordyng second commandement pryncypal aforesayd haue knowleche wete creature loueth neyghbour sayd comandement ought haue ij thynges wete euyl wel therfore sayd seuen comandementes partyculer fyrst enduceth excyteth creature wel hyt euery creature bounden doo wel neyghbour neuerthelesse moost bounden especyal doo good tho persones hym moost nygh moost conioyned therfore sayd fyrst comandement vij enduceth admonesteth creature wel comanded honoure serue ayde fader moder whiche ben persones moost conioynt v whome moost holden god suche honoure thy fader moder ende thou haue good longe lyf vpon erthe cause wherfore ought honoure faders moders grete benefaytes receyue iij thynges pryncypally first chylde receyueth fader moder beyng therfore chylde ought bere gretter honoure obeyssaunce ony god secondly chylde receyueth fader moder nourisshyng chyldehode therfore chylde bouden gouerne theyr olde age goodes admynystre vnto theyr necessytees power yf haue nede pthyrdly chylde receyueth fader moder techyng doctryne therfore al thynges ageynst god chylde oweth obeye thys doyng v thynges ben promysed god prophete chylde pfyrst grace world glorye perdurable secondly longe lyf ought nombred nombre yeres nombre good vertues lyf wythoute synne thyrdly ioye lygnage chyldren fourthly fame renommee lowable fyfthly rychesses wete somme sayd fader cause carnal generacyon many cause somme ben sayd fader eche ought bere honour reuerence fyrst sayd fader good holy doctryne good ensaumple haue gyuen shewed good holy lyf apostle sayntes holy doctryne haue maad v chyldren ihesu cryst feythe ouzt bere honour reuerence obeyssaunce onelye wyth mouthe ensyewyng theyr werkys theyr good holy lyues doctryne secondly ben sayd fader admynystracyon haue god lyke ben prelate holy chyrche whome ought gyue honoure obeyeng theyr comandements mynystres god p thyrdly somme sayd fader garde defence ought theyr people ben kyng prynce lordes whiche haue peple gouerne kepe ought loue honoure obeye subiectyon theyr power cometh god fourthly somme ben sayd fader ben honoured weel good receyued ben socour poure theyr necessyte fader pyte compassyon fyfthly somme sayd fader ought honoured theyr olde age peple whiche grete age sayd fyrst comandement partyculer touchyng loue dylectyon neyghbour whiche enduceth somoneth creature doo wel folowen vj whiche defende creature doo euyl therfore emonge alle euylles creature may another grettest euyl sle hym gyuen moyses second comandement vij thou shalte slee wete creature resonable thy propre wylle auctoryte knowleche whiche commandement wete holy scrypture slayn creature resonable many maners fyrst smytyng body hurtyng suche maner deth ensyeweth therof onely ageynst second commaundement pryncypal aforesayd whiche comandeth loue neyghbour hym self ageynst nature naturelly al thynges lyke semblable loue eche secondly gyuyng counceyl fauour ayde tenduce creature slee another bodyly make hym falle dedely synne thyrdly makyng comforte ayde creature slee another corpor lly cause hym falle dedely synne fourthly consentyng hym selfe bodely deth another spyrituel touchyng dedely synne make another falle whiche consentyng vnderstonde ofte tymes may lette another fro dethe corporel spyrytuel touchyng dedely synne lette hym appyereth clerely ynough creature somtyme sleeth body iniurye doon body suche wyse deth ensyeweth somtyme soule make falle dedely synne somtyme body soule togyder sleyng hym self woman grete wyth chylde lyuyng second comandement defendeth euyl persone conioyned maryage thys thou shalt none aduoultrye say wyth woman conioyned another maryage thou shalt haue noo comyxtyon flesshly companye ne woman also maryed wyth ony man hir husbond wete man woman doyng ageynst sayd comandement synne fyrst ayenst lawe god whiche hath defendyd aduoultrye sayd comandement yet synne ageynst lawe god whyche sayd whiche god hath conioyned maryage man may deceueryd ne departed gyuyng ouer body carnal copulacyon another holy scrypture man woman maryage ben constytuted weyne one flesshe yet efte synne ageynst sacrament maryage made face holy chyrche whiche man woman promytte theyr trouthe vertu whiche oth body man longeth woma body woman man ought abandouned ne delyuerd comyxtion carnal alweye wel thynges aforsayd synne dedely sayd yet synne woman abandouneth hyr body another man hir husbond companye carnal comyxtion gretter whan chyldren lygnage ensyeweth man wyth synnes aforsayd commytteth thefte gyuyng hyr husbond heyres succede hym another man hym self woma commytteth sacrelege trayson thefte caases synne man hath commysed aduoultrye reprehended woman cause ought haue gretter knowleche stronge kepe hym synne woman frayle deceyued lyghtly concupyscence also man ordeyned constytuted heed maystre woman doyng synne gyueth wyf euyl ensaumple also wete comandemet aforsayd onely deffended aduoultrye man woman assemblyd maryage al fornycacion comyxtion flesshly companye bytwene man woman lawful maryage dedely synne deffended sayd comandement holde contrarye heresye take aweye fro god gyuen consecrate holy sacrament baptesme gyue creature grete iniurye mysprysion gretter synne take fro creature thenne sythe defended suche vylo ye suche iniurye made creature strenger reason ought wyse doon vnto god also yet ageynst sayd comandement ne mespryseth onelye man woman aduoultrye fornycacyon touchyng dede fayte al tymes doo hyt haue wylle delyberyd concluded withoute dede doon folowe dedely synne also al byholdynges touchynges kyssynges made deliberacion come dede carnal comyetion fornycacion wel man woman maryage wihoute dede ensyewe dedely synne defended sayd commandement thyrd commandement defendeth euyl hurte another temporel goodes thou shalt thefte ageynst comandement myspryse synnen dedely al pryuely secretely take others goodes entencion reteyne ageynst wylle hym owe thys maner takyng thefte also al manyfestly openlye force vyolence taken goodes maner takyng callyd rauyne gretter dedely synne thefte synne fallen prynces lordes wythoute cause resonable leueye reyse vpon people tayllage aydes indue subuencyons auaryce maken euyl wycked ordynaunces vpon peple saynt austyn al wycked seygnourye thefte sayd saynt austyn suche peple suche lordes ben called grete theuys also al reteyne hyre salarye owe ayenst iustyce wyl euery man rendryd also fayt marchandyse delyberacyon dede aduysed commyse falsehed domage also tauerners sellars wyn put water wyn selle put lasse value lasse pry whiche vessel selle al one pry palso ayenst comandement mespryse synne alle doo vserye whiche commysed made many maners somtyme openlye wete whan creature leneth money another certeyn couenaunte shal haue prouffyte therby somtyme pryuely secretelye dyuers maners fyrst whan creature leneth another golde syluer thynge gretter surete payed ageyn delyuerd honde somme thynge cometh prouffyt ben medowys vygnes herytages yf receyue sayd prouffyt withoute wyl ony thynge rebate whiche lente secondly whan surete haue ageyne whyche hath lente persone hath receyued pledge hors beestes whome thusage hath doon hym prouffyte wyl thynge rebate therfore afore sayd thyrdly whan ostage delyuerd payement somme fynaunces therfore taketh despences vpon sayd ostages duryng tyme fourthly whan ony fynaunce due ony persone payement sayd fynaunce gyueth delaye certayn prouffyt made cause fyfthly whan creature accustomed bye retis thynges suche condycyon yf wyth incerteyn tyme hys money rendred ne payed ageyn shal haue thynge tyme sayd beyng byeth lasse worth seeth clerely hath solde hath ne shal haue terme power paye ne rendre whyche lente yf haue power thys hope wylle gyueth hym tyme rechate byeng ageyn thenne shal haue prouffyte thyng shal haue ageyn al hath lente wtthoute ony thynge abate therof also whan ony persone gyueth terme payement thynge hath solde abydyng payemynt hath solde derrer worthe value also whan creature byeth ony thynge shal delyuerd hym certeyn tyme come thabydyng delyueraunce thynge byeth lasse worthe also whan creature accompanyeth hym wyth another fayte marchaudyse delyuerth money suche couenaunte shal felowe partyner gayne bere thynge losse vpon caas vsure comprysed maner delyuer beestys deelyng shal deye whiche callyd beestys yron say supposed deye perysshe taketh moison delyng shal delyuer hem ageyn hath delyuerd shal bere noo parte losse gayne shal haue parte palso whan creature byeth ony rente reuenue thynge shal payed hym certeyn terme suche condycyon yf payed sayd terme shal gyue euery day euery weke somme thynge forberyng defaulte payement byerleueyeth receyueth sayd payne thynge also whan abyde payement lente hym oweth prest ette receyued seruyse werkys laboures bodely also ageynst sayd commandement mespryse synne dedely bye dygnytees espyrytuel benefyces al commyse symony also alle force tyrannye holden temporal seygnoryes lordshyppes al caases aforesayd creature holden restore al whiche hath receyued ony ageynst sayd comandement thre comandementes toforesayd defende doo euyl werke foloweth iiij deffendeth euyl hurtyng doyng wronge worde thou shalt speke ayenst thy neyghbour false wytnes ayenst comandement trespacen synnen mortalle al accusen fals iugement also al iudgen falsely also alle detraccon sayeng euyl take aweye good name fame also alle recyten taken playsyr delyte sayeng recountyng whiche haue herde saye recyte deffame also al alowe approuue wordes creature sayd deffame hym false doctryn ageynst trouthe faythe holy chyrche somtyme thynges domage gryef another touchyng goodes temporell two caases al lesynges foude dedely synne somtyme lesyng sayd commysed hys propre dede humylyte doon somme people accusen self confessyon humylyte whyche haue doon fro suche leesyng ought creature moche kepe hym ware right gretely therof suche humylyte wycked sayeng saynt austyn lyke creature ought hele ne hyde hys confessyon whyche hath doon lyke wyse ouzt say whyche hath doon psomtyme creature lyeth owne dede shame wete whan sayth somme thynge weneth trewe sayeng aduyseth hym knoweth hym self soo neuertheles shame dare wythdrawe hath sayd accordyng vnto trouthe pand somtyme creature lyeth haue somme prouffyte therby escape somme perylle somtyme doo prouffyte vnto another delyuer kepe hym somme perylle empesshe hys prouffyte lette hys dommage p also somtyme creature maken lesynges lye iapes playes gladde enioye people whyche companye wyth al pand fro alle lesynges sayeng swete saynt austyn creature ought alwaye kepe hym euery leesyng synne two fyrst ben dedely synnes thother euyl custo may bryng creature dedely synne iiij comandementes aforesayd whiche defende euyl werk worde folowe two whyche defende wylle lyberte greue euyl another fyrst deffendeth wylle hurte another goodes temporel thou shalte coueyte thynge thy neyghbour ayenst comandement mespryseth synneth creature somtyme mortally dedely wete ofte delyberacyon coueyteth wold haue goodes another ayenst reason somtyme venyally wete whan coueyteth goodes another wold haue reason pry worthe good wylle hym owe second commandement defendeth wylle delybered concluded coueyte wyf another man haue carnal companye wyth hir haue knowleche sayd comandemet vnderstonde iij maners concupyscence carnal creature fyrst herte whan consentyng delybered concluded purpoos sayth sauyour ihesu cryst byholdeth woman carnal concupyscence say wylle concluded haue hyr companye flesshly herte hath commysed fornycacyon synneth dedely secondly mouth expressyng declaryng theuyl desyre hert consentyng whych consetyng called dedely synne thyrdly werke whan euyl purpoos consetyng done dede wete iiij thynges pryncipally kepe creature fro fallyng synne concupyscence p fyrst flee euyl companye alle occasyons gyuen moeuen cause concupyscence frequente see wymmen ofte speke ij put remembre herte euyl thouztes temptacions come thynges hath seen chastyse body holde penauce afflictio iij haue recours god deuoute oryson prayer whan flesshly temptacyon cometh requyryng deuoutlye helpe pthe sayth sawe beest yssued oute see merueyllously desgysed moche dredeful body beest lyepard foot beer throte lyo vij heedes x horne aboue aboue x horne x crownes saynt iohan sawe cruel beest hath power myght fyghte ayenst sayntes ouercome conquere thys beest cruel conntrefayted dyuers dredeful signefyeth deuyl helle ful sorow al bytternesse body beest sayth saynt iohan semblaunte vnto lyepard lyke wyse lyepard hath dyuers colour lyke wyse hath deuyl dyuers maners engynes deceyue drawe peple synne foot beest bere lyke wyse beer hath myght strengthe foot armes holdeth strongly byclyppeth fast whiche hath vnder foot enbraceth lyke wyse doeth deuyl embraceth hath beten doun synne throte lyon hym grete cruelte vij hedes sayd beest ben vij chyef dedely synnes deuyl draweth hym al world oftyme happeth many sone falle throte vij hedes vnderstonde seuen dedely synnes therfore sayth saynt iohan sayd beest power ayenst saynces erthe none holy man parfytelye may eschewe al maners synnes vij heedes vij dedely synnes descende withoute specyal pryuylege grace god lyke virgyn marie whyche neuer dyd synne another saynt specyal grace god lyke gloryous vyrgyn marye specyal synguler grace god aboue al creature x horne beest sygnefye brekyng x commandementes lawe lord whych deuyl pourchaceth moche may creature breke lyke wyse purchaceth creature falle vij dedely synnes toforesayd braunches x crownes sayd beest sygnefyen vyctoryes deuyl hath vpon synners cause hath made breke ten comandements lawe lord herafter foloweth deuysyon vij dedely synnes ca xiij fyrst heed beest pryde second enuye iij yre wrath iiij slouthe v auaryce vj glotonnye vij lecherye oute vij synnes dedely descenden alle maner synnes therfore callyd chyef vyces ben chyef al vyces alle synnes dedely venyal eueryche seuen dedely synnes departed many partyes first shal speke synne pryde first synne begynnyng al euyl whan angel lucyfer grete beaute grete vnderstondyng wold haue ben aboue alle angel wold compare god good fayr made hym cause took suche pryde hym fyl fro heuen helle became deuyll alle hys companye wyth hym alle proude men resemble thys lucyfer whiche wyl aboue preysed allowed enhaunced whiche better valewe synne pryde ouer perylous blyndeth man woman knowe ne see perylle wherin synne right stronge wyn deuyl moost especyal enyureth maketh dronke grete lordes ladyes bourgeyses ryche noble valyaunte persones generally al maner people especyal grete lordes ladyes suche maner knowe self ne see theyr defaultes ne theyr folyes ne theyr synnes thys moost perylous maladye sekenesse al certeynly grete peryl whome alle tryacle torneth venym lyke doctryne chastysyng doth proude men chastyse blame theyr defaultes moche ben angry defende pryde fyrst doughter deuyl hath moost grettest parte herytage pryde warreth ageynst god goodnes al grace ageyn al good werkys ben pryde maketh almesse synne vertu vyce thus pryde theef god wyth goodes one ought gete heuen maketh hym wynne helle synne fyrst assaulteth knyghtes lord laste leueth whan knyghtes god haue ouercomen vaynquysshed alle vyces synnes thenne assaulte strongly synne pride vayne glorye pthe brauches synne pryde ben capo xiiij synne pride deuydeth hym departeth many partyes vnnethe may nombred ben synne vij pryncypal partyes whiche seuen braunches yssue growe euyl rote whyche fyrst braunche pryde dysloyalte vntrouthe second despyte thyrd surquydrye whiche calle presumpcion fourth folehaste whiche called ambycion fyfthe vayne glorye vj ypocrysye vij euyl foule shame wel doyng vij partyes braunches apperteyne alle synnes growe pryde eueryche vij braunches haue many smale bowes pthe first braunche dysloyalte vntrouthe capo xv fyrst brauche pryde dysloyalte whiche deuydeth hym thre braunches first euyl second werse thyrd werste one vylaynnous wode thyrd renyeng vylaynnous generally alle synnes noo synne wythoute vylonye vylonye whiche speke specyally groweth pryde partye dysloyalte whyche called clerkes ingratytude vnkyndenes say forgetyng god yeftes men thanke lord ne yeue hym laude praysyng therof forgeteth rendreth euyl good vylonye curtesye vylonye doth euery creature god whan forgeteth goodnes grace yeftes yeldeth hym therfore praysynges thankes lyke ought oftymes fyghteth euyl custome vsage ageynst wylle god moche grete vylonye whan persone receyueth grete bounte goodnes daygneth one say gramercy yet vylanye gretter whan one seeth whan forgeteth slouthe ouer grete whan persone receyueth alle waye bountees rendreth alwaye euyl good thenne bethought hym wel took hede ofte bountees goodes god hath gyuen doon hym doeth contynuelly fro day day hath noo goodes god hath gyuen hym ne goodes nature beaute helthe strengthe body clere vnderstondyng natural wytte partye soule ne goodes fortune lyke rychesses honoures hawtesses ne goodes grace lyke ben vertues grace good werkes wel ought suche persone preyse thanke god honoure doubte loue hym wyth al goodes one bounte requyreth asketh another pof second bough first braunche capo xvj second bough dysloyaulte groweth pryde woodnes holden wood oute wytte whome reason goon departed thene ryght grete fool wel may sayd oute wytte wood good ernest wasteth destroyeth setteth euyl vsage goodes ben ben goodes lord whiche must straytely counte gyue rekenyng th wete tyme hath loste hath em loyed tyme temporelle goodes hath vsed whiche hath kepyng hath despended folyes oultrages euyl vsages tofore eyen lord god ne hath pourueyed hym rendre acompte knoweth wel muste rekene wote whenne ne day ne houre suche folye callyd forsenerye woodnesse thys vyce thys synne grete proude men vse ryght euyl goodes god hath lente pof thyrd bowh dysloyaulte capitulo xvij thyrd bowhe dysloyaulte cometh pryde renyeng wel renyed lode despyte whiche moche grete synne wel dedely synne wythoute despyte god yet alwey speke despyte specyally may one synne thre maners cause persone preyseth ryghtfully another herte lyke ought cause bereth reuerence ne honoure ouzt cause obeyeth ryght whome ought obeye pnow thynke ryght wel dylygently thyn herte oftymes thou hast mesprysed herin whyche thou hast thyn herte thyn owne self falsely preysed bettyr despreysed despyted werse preysed thynke hou ofte thou hast despysed thyn herte ben valewe tha thou arte thou hast despysed forayne grace god hath gyuen noblesse beaute prowesse strengthe body lyghtnes someuer good whyche thou hast preysed thy self thou oughtest thou hast lasse preysed thou oughtest thynke hou many tymes thou hast borne lytel honour reuerence thou oughtest fyrst god swete moder alle angel sayntes heuen none thou hast trespaced despyte irreuerence thou hast ofte tymes euyl kepte festys holy dayes thynke hou many tymes thou hast seruyd euyl lord ihesu cryste thou hast gladly herde seruyce ne sayd houres ne herde sermon whan thou wenest messe chyrche sermon thou ianglest bourdest tofore god lettest wel thynke thou hast many tymes doon lytel honour body ihesu cryste whan thou seest hym whan thou receyuest hym thys thou arte worthely apparaylled ne made redy confessyon repentaunce aduenture werse thou hast receyued hym dedely synne thy self wytyng whiche thynge grete despyte vnto god crucyfye hym thynke vnto thy swete felowe thy good kep r thyn angel whiche alwaye wyth alwaye kepeth many vylanyes thou hast doon hym soo moche thou hast commysed synne tofore hym thynke oftymes thou hast inobedyent thy fader thy moder whome thou oughtest obeye bere honour yf thou wylt manere recorde thy lyf thou shalte see thou hast ofter synned maner pryde whyche called despyte thou canst recounte telle iij braunche pryde arrogance capo xix thyrd braunche pryde arrogance callyd surquydrye presumpcyon wete whan man weneth hym self oughte say weneth valewe power knowe daygneth doo thother doo whiche ben valewe also wyl synguler werkys fyrst synne whiche surquydrye sheweth hym werke dede second folye enterpryse grete dyspences owen preysed renomed holden large curtoys thyrd euyl groweth surquydrye folysshe empryse leude stryffe thus sayth salamon emonge proude men alwaye stryues plees iiij bough thys braunche whyche proude man sheweth pryde flatre vauntours losengers suffre preyse say durst say lye crye theyr oublyes fyfthe tacke braunche derisyon custom proude surquydrous suffyseth ynough despyse herte hath grace weneth haue maketh mockeryes derysyons yet werse scorneth mocketh good wyse men seeth good honeste whyche moche grete synne perylous euyl tongue lette moche peple wele vj boughe thys braunche rebellyon whan man rebelle alle wold hym good yf one repreue proude surquydrous deffendeth hym yf one chastyse hym anone angry yf one counceyl hym byleueth hys owne wytte peryllous maladye may suffre touched whome euery medycyne torneth venym hit euyl thynge murmure moche werse rebellyon rebellyon vyce herte whiche harde froward dyuers wyl alwaye wylle doon sentence holden wyl alle bowe enclyne hym shal bowe ne rebellyon departeth deuydeth hym four braunches suche herte repugnante rebelle byleue counceyl suffre chastysyng receyue doctryne yf ony theyr frendes wold counceyl shewe theyr prouffyte theyr defaultes deygneth take hede therto ne cause haue spoken wyl gladly al contrarye party moche rebelle counceylles lord counceyl holy gospellys holy scryptures sermon whiche bounden accomplysshe wylle god haue glorye perdurable deuyl leyeth tofore eyther impotence yongthe age euyl reason laste may thynge doo wha men repreue chastyse defende boor wyl knowe theyr folyes moche excuse moche theyr synne also wha god smyteth chastyseth correcteth hem ende shold knowe theyr synnes theyr defaultes ende repente amende con hym noo thanke despyse hym sayeng haue trespaced wyl god doo wyth thus murmure persone hath many venymous thoughtes fals demynges iugementes may nombred thys whan enuyous persone dooth hereth ony euyl ony someuer hyt harme body euyl hys deth hys sekenesse euyl fortune pouerte aboute hym braunche growe vj bowes whan ire ryseth bytwene two men thene stryf dyscorde wordes vylonyes wronges rancour whyche dwellyth herte cometh hate medlyng bataylle desyre tauenge hym otherwhyle homycyde manslaughter cometh ofte mortalle warre emonge frendes whiche yssuen ofte euyls dyuers maners many may amended whan warre bytwene two hye grete men hyt happeth ofte many men slayn whyche maners synnes fyrst vyce fayntnes whan man loueth lytyl fayntly lord whome oweth loue ardantly happeth whan flawe latchous slowful wel second vyce slouthe tendrenesse bedde wherin deuyl resteth hym annoyeth hym lyue hym self desyreth deth p al sorouful poyntes slouthe gyueth deuyl mortal stroke putteth hym despayr whiche hym self purchaceth deth sleeth hym self ellys playeth wyth hym self lyke moche penaunce byhoueth ypocryte haue ij mesures one lytel one grete vse lytel mesure tofore peple grete mesure vse man see reteyne trewe mesure ben auaricio suche maner mouth wyl lady hous comandour thenne bytwene bely mouth gloton ben thre dysputacyons bely sayth wolde ful mouth saith wyl ful bely saith hym wyl thou ete take ynough despende largely mouth sayth shal wyl thou restrayne shal sory caytyf seruaunt two euyl lordes two mesures maken pee mesure bely man hous good large mesure mouth owen hous sorouful ouer ar pthey lyuen physyque kepen mesure ypocras whyche lytel streyte happeth oft lyueth physyke deyeth pthey lyuen honeste kepe holde mesure rayson lyuen honourably world eten tyme houre taken gree worth whyche haue curtoyslye clenly gladlye lyue theyr synne requyreth kepe suche mesure charged penaunce lyue spyrite ben loue god rule gouern hem self lyke holy ghoost enseygneth techeth holde kepe mesure reason ordre haue lordshyp seygnorye ouer theyr body whiche dysciplyned endoctryned penaunce wel chastysed demaundeth none oultrage doeth whiche spyrite commaundeth wythoute contradyction mayst thou see whiche haue sayd deuyl hath many engynes take peple theyr throtes theyr glotonye fyrst sheweth wynes mete ben fayr delycyouses lyke dyd eue apple yf worthe sayth hym ete drynke lyke dyd suche one thou must nedes holde companye wylt thou men mocke scorne wylte thou ben holden popelard sayth thou must nedys kepe helthe thy body hath helth hath thynge homycyde thy self thou owest thy body sustenaunce sayth hym otherwyse beholde consydere good thou doest thou mayst thou etest delytes thy body serue god thou oughtest kepe thy strengthe god lyke dauyd prophete sayth reason abouesayd somtyme atteyned deceyued moost wyse men thyrd braunche vyce renne take ouer gredyly mete lyke hounde dooth caroyn moche gretter gredynesse soo moche gretter synne lyke synne haue rychesse iustely goten truly ouer moche loue ne vse euyl right synne ete ouer gredely ne ouer dysordynatly al manere mete ben good vnto good people reason mesure vsen without ony excesse without oultrage alwey ouzt preyse god rendre thakynges god goodnes yeftes swetenes mete ouzt thynke swetenesse god celestyal swete mete glorye perdurable fylleth accomplyssheth desyre hert therfore men rede howses religyon mete cause whan body taketh refection one parte soule shold take spyrituel mete refection part iiij braunche synne glotonye ouer nobly wyl ete drynke despende waste wherof hondred poure men myght suffycietly fedde suche peple synne many maners fyrst grete despences make vse ouer grete gredynes ouer grete delyte vayn glorye haue onelye thexcesse throte ofte bobance grete pryde praysyng world seche dere mete multeplye many mess wherof oft tymes growe many synnes v brauche glotonye curiosite glotons whiche thynke none thynge delyte mete ben proprelye lychorous seche sauf onely delytes theyr throte mouth iij thynges namely lyeth synne suche peple fyrst grete charge haue pourchasyng arayeng mete glorye grete playsyr haue seyng beholdyng may recounte dylygence put mete wel arayed eueryche haue right propre saw e may one thynge make dyuers mess dysguysed delycyousnesse mouthe whan messys mete come one another thene sayd bourdes entremesses thus goeth tyme caytyfs forgete self reason slepeth thynketh thynge deth ne synnes stomack cryeth sayth dame throte ye slee ful lyke breke thene lychorous tongue answereth though thou sholdest brest shal suffre licoro mete escape lycorones mete cometh vaynglory remebre thene desyre wesshe longe necke crane grete bely cowe myght yet deuoure swalowe mete hast thou herde synnes comen glotonye lycourousnesse cause synnes sourden comen ofte tauerne whiche fontayne synne therfore wyl lytel touche synnes ben made done tauerne tauerne scole deuyl dyscyples studye propre chapel seruyce doon place sheweth doeth myracles bothe day nyght suche apperteynen deuyl atte chyrche lord god hath custome shewe vertues make myracles lyke ye may see many place blynde see lame croked redressyd mad men wytte dombe men speche deef men theyr heryng deuyl tauern doth al contrarye tauerne chapel aforesayd men dooth hym seruyce whan man goeth tauerne goeth alle ryght whan retorneth hath neyther fote ne honde whyche may hym self bere ne susteyne whan goeth thyder speketh wel hereth vnderstondeth whan retorneth hath loste alle thys lyke hath neyther wytte ne reason ne memorye hym self suche myracles deuyl maketh tauerne lesson redde tauerne shal say ther redde lerned herde seen fylthe ordure synne wete glotonye lecherye sweryng forsweryng lyeng myssayeng renyeng god sayntes mysherkenyng brawlyng many synnes thene sourden comen stryues homycides manslaughter lernyd stele hange tauern fosse pytte theuys also fortresse deuyl warre ayenst god sayntes tauerner susteyneth suche peple dysordynate ben partonners alle theyr synnes doo theyr tauernes certeyn yf persone sayd moche shame hys owne fader moder knaue suche manere peple theyr fader heuen lady sayntes shold moche angry fynde sette remedye god dooth pof synnes tongue capitulo l wyl knowe thynke synnes tongue hym byhoueth thynke acounte thynk tongue fro whens cometh harme euyl doeth happeth somtyme worde synne hym self cause euyl happeth cause synne men synne moche yssueth cometh euyl herte pand also happeth worde grete synne cause dooth euyl wel fayre wel polysshed pnow thou oughtest knowe euyl tongue tree god curseth gospel cause fonde theron thynge leeuys leeuys ben vnder stonden holy scrypture wordes lyke shold thynge dyffycile harde nombre leeuys tree ryght impossyble compte nombre synnes growen tongue shal sette put ten chyef braunches whyche growe oute thys tree x braunches may thus named ydlenes auauntyng losangerye detraction lye lesynges forswerynges contencyons murmure rebellyon blasphemye pof synne ydle wordes capo lj abandone ydle wordes geten grete dommage grete perylle whyche apperceyue pand also lese tyme whyche may neuer recouere lose also good dedes shold myght doo vnto theyr owne salute helthe lesen ioye heuen tresour theyr herte replenysshe vanyte synnes dyscouer potte flyes entre therin calle ydle wordes ben ben moche costyous damageous perillous auoyde fro herte al goodnes replenysshe wyth vanyte shal rendre reason yelde acompt god straytely atte day iugement lyke god saith gospel thenne lytel thynge ne lytel ydlenes whan hit byhoueth yelde reason accomptes day dome vnto lytel thought hye court tofore god al sayntes ydle wordes men synne vj maners somme vayn wordes whyche somme tongue ful moche speke afore lyke clyket clappe mylle whyche may neuer reste also wordes ben soo curyous gladly heren tydynges tolde ofte sette theyr hert desease recounters ofte holden fooles lyars comen rehersayl fayr wordes wherin moche vaynglorye subtylly shewe say make herars laughe ben truffes bourdes lye ful fylthe ordure synne whiche ben callyd ydle wordes peryllous greuable ben iapes esbatemens playes leeful say somtyme vpon good men vpon wold fayn wel cause myght wythdrawe fro theyr herte goodnes haue conceyued purpose ydle wordes thou art lyke homycyde yf thou wythdrawe thy tongue man woman chylde fro doyng wel fro doyng good dede god shal conne good thanke kyng shold yf thou haddest slayn owne sone stolen aweye hys tresour pof synne auauntance capitulo lij cometh synne auauntyng whych moche grete moche foule false moche vylaynous moche grete auauteth hym self moche hateful god taketh awaye glorye also haue sayd tofore moche false synne goodes myzt gete heuen gyueth lytel wynde soo moche foule synne al world holdeth hym fool vylayn nyce braunche hath v leuys ben v maners vauntours one tyme past thys synne gladly remembre theyr werkys theyr prowess whyche wene haue done wel sayd wel tyme present synne thynge gladly ne payne doo wel ne say wel whan seen ne herde doyng sayeng syngyng auaunte self selle nouzt alle haue doon man apperteyneth synne auaunte boost good haue whyche wene haue theyr noblesse theyr rychesse ben lyke cuckow synge hym self p thyrd ben surquydrous thynke say self shal auenge herof shal make hylles valeyes fourth subtyl dare preyse self shame al euer doon say blame despyse lyke thynge worth whyche doo say p fyfthe yet subtyl wyl whan men preyse dare saye openlye make contrarye make self humble say thynge worth synners thre tymes wers cause wold preysed men shold holde wel humble meke ala sayth saynt bernard sorouful auauntynge make theym selfe deuylles cause shold reputed aungellys fayne self euyl thende men shold repute good certeynly man shold angre say ye say trouthe apperteyneth synne sechen aduocates preyse crye theyr oublyes who mouth speke hardely pof euyl sayeng capitulo liij losangers ben nouryces deuyl gyue souk chyldren make slepe theyr synnes theyr fayre syngyng enoynte waye helle wyth hony flaterye cause synners shold goo hardely synne departed fyue partyes lyke fyue leuys braunche fyrst flaterers whan see see dyspose say wel wel anone shewe telle hym cause shold haue therof vayn glorye defaultes shal neuer say ne telle hym second synne lytel good chyldren double say preyse fede flaterye encreace double adiouste therto soo moche lesyng trouthe therfore callyd false wytnesse holy scrypture p thyrd synne whan make man woman vnderstonde hath hym many good vertues moche grace hath none therfore holy scrypture calleth suche flateres enchautours enchaunte moche man woman byleue better hem self byleue bettyr whiche see saye hem better knowe fele pthe fourth synne whan synge alwaye placebo flaterye say lord lady ye say trouthe lord doth wel torneth al thynge flaterye someuer doeth sayth good euyl therfore ben callyd ecko n redoundeth hye mountayns woodes accordeth alwaye whiche cryed sayd trewe fals fyfthe ben flaterers defenden excusen couere vyces synnes wyl flatere preyse therfore ben callyd wrytyng taylles couer ordure synnes ryche men somme temporal good therfore ben lykenyd scrypture tayll foxe theyr flaterye barate tryeherye pof losengerye flaterye losengiers myssayers ben one soole ben ij seraynes otherwyse callyd mermaydes whiche fynde book nature beestys whiche monstre see callyd serayns whyche hath body woman taylle fysshe vngles clawes egle synge soo swetely make maronners slepe deuoure ben losengyers flaterers whiche theyr fayr speche make men slepe theyr synnes somme serpentes whyche haue name serayns renne swyftely hors somtyme flee theyr venym stronge tryacle may auayle ayenst sonner cometh deth bytyng serpent felte ben myssayers whome salamon sayth byte trayson lyke serpent thys ben slayn thre one sayth hereth whome myssayed ryght cruel beest callyd hate whiche fynyssheth destroyeth bryngeth erth bodyes dede men eteth ben byte ete good men relygyon ben world suche manere peple ben cruel helle deuoureth wycked peple renne vpon good deuoureth suche maner peple resemblen sowe whiche whan hath pygges gladly wyl byte man clad whyt clothes ben lyke huppe maketh nest ordure man resteth hym lyke dorre waspe flee floures louen dunge ordure branche hath fyue leuys fyrst whan contryue lesynges euyl hurte blame defame second whan haue herde blame harme say forth reporte peple adiouste self therto thyrd whan quenche sette nought alle good man hath doon make holden euyl ete man al hole ete hym alle byte hym bere aweye pyece pthis fourth leef braunche whiche proprely called detraction alway wythdraweth cutteth pyece good hereth spoken whan ony good spoken ony tofore hym alwaye contryueth somthynge saye reproche gyueth therto thus ryght good man loue hym wel ben suche defaultes hym certaynly sory therfore scorpyo blandyssheth wyth face prycketh wyth hys taylle fyfthe whan peruerteth torneth al wers partye good euyl therfore false iuge vntrewe pof synne say lesynges capitulo liiij lesyng falseth man lyke one falsed seal kyng bulles pope cause suche men falsen money beren forth false letter shal iuged day dome false man lyar emonge good trewe men fals peny emonge good chaffe emonge corne lyar lyke deuyl whiche fader lyke god sayth gospel lyar fader lesynges forged fyrst lesynge yet forgeth techeth forth alle day deuyl sheweth hym many maners many fourmes transfygureth hym self many guy deceyue people ryght soo dooth lyar thenne lyke plouyer whyche lyueth wynde ayer hath thynge hys entraylles wynde also euery colour seeth chaungeth sowne braunche thre bowes one manere leesyng brennyng another playsaunt another noyeng alle thre synne lyke sayth saynt austyn wel lyeth wyth hys lesyng doth good prouffyte another neuerthelesse doth owne hurte domage thenne lye ardaunt ben synnes lye playsaunte ben gretter synne lyke ben lye losengiers flaterers mynystrellis trufars whyche sayen bourdes lesynges derysyons solace folke make laughe doubte take hede synne lesynges greuyng noyeng ben dedely synne whan sayd ernestlye wyth thought harme hurte ony pto braunche apperteynen al falsetees fallaces deceytes guylles ben doon sayd thorugh oute al world deceyue hurte ony soule body hauour renome fame pof synne forsweryng capo lv euyl lye moche werse gretter synne man forswere hym self peryllous thynge forswere hym self therfore lord deffendeth moche cause one may wyse swere wythout synne ofte swere maketh man often forswere hym ofte synne vij maners may man synne makyng othes fyrst whan one swereth ardauntly despyte gladly lyke semeth delyteth fro hym self ptherfore defendeth saynt iames onely swere whan nede wylle swere also whan one swereth nought nought whan one swereth lyghtly wythoute cause wythoute reason deffended second commaundement lawe whiche god wrote table stoon wyth blessyd fyngre delyuerd moyses prophete preche peple pafter whan one swereth accustomably lyke many doon euyl taught noo thynge say wythoute sweryng swere ny none thynge calle god wytnesse cause ought moche grete resonable trewe shold called dare calle soo grete lord god wytnesse gloryous moder sayntes also whan one swereth folyly cometh happeth many maners swereth yre sodaynly whiche whan repreued repenteth anone wha one swereth thyng whiche may kepe wythout synne suche swerynges ought lefte penaunce folysshe oth whan one swereth certeynly thynge whyche certayn wel trewe whan one swereth certaynly whiche knoweth may accomplysshe whan one swereth creature say sonne shyneth fyre breneth heed soule fader suche semblable thynges god deffendeth al othes gospel whiche ought conferme ought take wytnesse souerayn trouthe god whiche knoweth al thynge pure creature whiche thynge vanytees whan men swere ernestly dyshonour god thonour god ought alweye kept al thynges whan men swere holy gospellys men swere hym whome wordes ben wryton whan one swereth holy relykes sayntes heuen swere god enhabyteth whan one swereth vylaynsly god sayntes ben crysten men werse sarasyns ne sweren manere ne suffren ony swere vylaynsly tofore ihesu lyke crysten men doo swereth theyr lawe mahomet theyr god shal stoned crysten men thys cruel iewes crucefyed ihesu cryst brake none bone swere hym rende make moo pyeces hym made beest boucherye many false cristen men lyke wyse breke pyeces blessyd lady sayntes sweryng vylaynslye certeynly merueyle cryst may suffre pafter whan one swereth falsely bereth false wytnesse wytyng ony maner swereth couertly openlye arte colour sophym lawe wryton sayth god loueth symplesse trouthe suche thynge receyueth oth vnderstondeth word say entende whiche symply wythoute barate vnderstonde moche grete debonayrte god whan suche men swere whyche knowe wel trouthe promytteth thynge whyche wyl holde deuyl strangle anone whan say god kepe god wyl helpe putteth hym self grace god ayde helpe ought veray ryght lese wytte mynde alle holde god pthe last braunche synne whan one breketh feyth hath promysed creanted fayth oth fayth lyed oth broken alle one pof synne peryll chydyng capitulo lvj saynt austyn sayth none lyke deuyl chydar thys crafte wythoute doubte pleseth moche deuyl dysplayseth moche vnto god whyche loueth aboue al thynges pee concorde braunche departeth hym vij bowes first stryue second chyde thyrd ledenger fourth curse fyfthe reproche repreue sixte menace threte seuenth dyscorde r yse hate whan deuyl seeth pee loue bytwene two persones moche desplayseth hym make dyscorde dooth hys power make stryue whan begynne stryue deuyl begynneth blowe syre angre thenne stryffe angre cometh noyse chydyng thenne fyre lyght smoke vp anone cometh flamme lepeth stryuyng whan one sayth chydyng whan demene say one grete wordes cometh ledanges whan pynche shoue one say grete vylanyes grete felonyes somme felous haue theyr tongue cuttyng rasour percyng arowes alles suche folke resemble porpyn whiche al ful pryckes sharpe poyntures ouer felle angry whan wrothe launceth casteth prickes lyke arowes oute body throweth ryght syde lyfte syde palso resembleth felon mastyf byteth barketh al seeth goo waye comen curse maledyctios whan one curseth grete synne scrypture sayth curseth neygbour cursed god pand saynt poul sayth suche folke may haue royame god salamon sayth theyr mouthes ben lyke pot boylleth casteth oute al sydes scaldeth aboute hym comen reproches whych ben yet synne whan man reprocheth another hys synnes defaultes folyes pouerte poure kynne defaultes hath hym wexyth angry synneth comen menace thretenynges thenne begynne medlynges warres aboue alle synnes haue named passeth synne theyr wycked tongue areyse moeue dyscordes deuysyons euyl wylle emonge frendes gyder destourbe lette pee accordes god hateth moche suche peple sayth scrypture pof synne murmure capitulo lvij see happeth ofte tyme dare answere ne chyde begynne murmure grunte wyth teeth therfore synne chydyng sette synne murmure moche synne grete god taketh vengeaunce correction shalle shewe god oftymes hath taken vengeaunce suche lyke holy scrypture recordeth erthe opened swolowed dathan abyron descended quycke helle synne god sente fyre heuen brente chore al felowes wete ij hondred xl thousand grettest hoost lord deserte synne loste iewes londe promyssyon whyche god promysed vjc thousand god delyuerd put seruage kyng egypt pharao nourisshed xl yere deserte wyth manna heuen al entryd holy londe promyssyon two persones onelye whiche named caleph iosue al deyed wyth sorow deserte synne hath two braunches murmure ayenst god somme ayenst man synne murmure ayenst man many maners lyke seruautes ayenste theyr lordes maysters chamberers wymmen ayenst theyr ladyes maystresses chyldren ayenst fader moder poure ayenst ryche vylaynes ayenst noble laye peple ayenst clerkes ayenst prelate cloysterers ayenst thabbottes pryours fy er murmure groweth ayenst persones inobedyence cause made ouer harde commandementes drede inpacience cause alle thynges doon ryghtfully enuye felonnye cause one auauced another many euyl rancour pmurmure ayenst god hath many occasion loste grace pacience wold god suche hynge god hath made erthe yf hath made wylle anone grutcheth ayenst god syngeth deuyls pater noster lyke holy ghoost enseygneth techeth chosen synge theyr herte swete songe heuen deo gracias al hath made gyuen v al sendeth v lyke wyse wycked spyrite maketh dyscyples synge songe helle murmure alwaye shal dure helle certeyn suche man moche fool wood wyl god shold gyue hym acomptes alle hath made yf sende hym pouerte maladye dere tyme yf take fro one gyue another al doon deuyse anone taketh ayenst god murmureth ayenst hym hym maulgree meruayle hit though god auenge hym suche folke whan wold take fro hym seygnorye sapyence puyssaunce pof synne perylle rebellyon capo lviij evyl thynge murmure moche euyl rebellyon rebellyon vyce cometh fro hert whiche harde froward dyuers alwaye wyl wylle doon sentence holden wyl humble bowe hym wyl bowe ne enclyne man herte dyuers salamon sayth may faylle euyl ende lyke murmure ayenst god ayenst man ryght soo suche hert rebelle ayenst god man vyce hath iiij braunches suche herte froward rebelle byleue counseyl taccomplysshe comandements god suffre chastysyng receyue doctryne vyce thou hast herde chappytre pryde pof synne blasphemye capo lix blasphemye sayth saynt austyn moche groweth c seche al condycions chappytre pryde tofore wryton rubyche arrogaunce ende haue shewed x maners synne tongue whiche fyrst ydle wordes last blasphemye salamon sayth begynnyng euyl tongue folye ende shal ouer euyl fynysshe thene dedely synnes al braunches descende knowe ye trouthe shold wel studye thys book myght wel prouffyte lerne knowe al maner synnes confesse hym self wel none may confesse synnes wel yf ne knowe hem thou oughtest knowe redeth book ought thynke take hede dylygently yf culpable ony synnes aforesayd yf fynde hym culpable ony ought repente hym anone confesse hym dylygently kepe hym hys power fro synnes whyche culpable also ought preyse thanke god humbly praye hym deuoutelye wyl kepe hym swete grace phow lyf ny deth hit appereth capo lx greuously dyeth hath lerned deye lerne thene dye yf thou shal conne lyue man shalle lyue hath lerned dye ryzt callyd caytyf lyue ne knoweth dye yf thou wylt lyue frely surelye lerne deye wyselye yf thou saye shal lerned shal telle thou oughtest knowe lyfnys deth deth departyng thys knoweth euery man therfore sayd man whan dyeth departeth whan deed departed lyfnys noo thynge departyng ye truly moche shorte departyng al lyf man yf lyued thousand yere onelye momet regarde lyf alwaye dureth torment ioye durable wytnesseth v kynges duke erles prynces emperours whiche somtyme glorye thys world p wepe helle crye howle cratchen sayen ala auaylled v power honour noblesse ioye beaultees al rychessys sone al thys departed faylled shadowe smoke moche faster fledde fro v byrdes fleyng quarelles oute crosse bowe thus departeth aweye lyf anone ben deed alle lyf lytel moment perdurable tormentes ioye wepyng carolles feestes sorowe roobes hoodes feestes dygnytees game rychessys al welthes ben faylled v suche songes helle lyke holy wrytte recounteth shewe v lyf thynge departyng thys dethe thynge departyng lyue thynge departe thenne lyuyng world noo thynge deye trewe pater noster whan thou beganst lyue anone thou beganst deye approche deth al thyn age alle thy tyme whiche passed deth hath conquerd reteyned thou saeyst thou hast xl yere trouthe deth hath ne neuer shal yelde ageyn therfore wytte world folye certayn clerkys seyng seen noo thynge al day uyght done one thynge lasse knowe alwaye deyen deye nyght day thou deyest haue sayd yet another maner shal teche clergye thende thou know wel lyue wel deye take hede vnderstonde deth thynge deceueryng body soule knoweth wel euery man vnderstondeth techeth v cathon wyse man lerne sayth deye departe deceuere oft thy soule thy spyryte fro thy body lyke dyd many grete phylosophres moche hated lyf despysed world moche desyred deye slewe self theyr owne agrement auaylled thynge grace ne faythe lord ihesu cryst holy men whiche loue god drede hym thre dethes haue passed tweyne ben deed touchyng synnes deed touchyng world abyde last deth thyrd deceueraunce soule body bytwene heuen lytel walle passe thought desyre though body world syde herte spyryte syde world theyr conuersacion heuen lyke sayth saynt poule theyr solace theyr ye theyr consolacion thought ferther syde heuen theyr conuersacion lyke sayth saynt poule therfore hate theyr lyf whyche deth desyre bodely deth damoysel bereth ioye deth whiche crowneth al sayntes sette ioye perdurable deth good man ende al euyllys yate entre al goodes deth ryuer departeth deth lyf deth syde lyf syde also wyse men world whiche ben thys syde ryuer world seen soo clere syde see noo thynge therfore callyd scrypture fooles blynde thys dethe calle departyng deth comune good callen ende therfore hate soo moche deth knowe ne syde ryuer haue conuersed ne knowe thynge gooeth oute thenne yf thou wylt knowe good euyl yssue thy self yssue oute world lerne deye dysseuere thy soule fro thy body thought sende thyn hert world heuen helle purgatorye shalte thou see good euyl pin helle thou shalte see mo sorowes dyuers tormentys ony man may deuyse ony herte thynke purgatorye also thou shalte see moo tormentes ony may endure heuen thou shalt see ioye glorye ony may desyre helle shal shewyd enseygned god vengeth dedely synne purgatorye shal shewe enseygne god purgeth dedely synne pin heuen thou shalte see clerely vertues good werkys hyely ben guerdoned rewarded thre thynges vnderstonde alle byhoueth knowe lyue wel deye wel phow men lyue dyeng world capo lxj beholde take hede yet lytel ennoye ne greue thre thynges therfore know wylle hate synne forgete thy body one tyme day goo helle lyuyng thende thou goo thyder thy deth thus doon ofte good men wyse thou shalte see alle herte hateth colde hete hungre thyrst dyuers tormentes wepynges syghes wayllynges hert may thynke ne tongue deuyse alle waye shal endure without ende therfore payne right called deth perdurable alway deth lyuyng lyf deyeng whan thou shalt see thene one dedely synne must nedys dere bouzt thou haddest leuer flayne al quyck tofore thou sholdest consente doo one onely synne goo purgatorye shalt thou see paynes soules haue repentaunce theyr synnes world parfytely purged make remenaute theyr penannce vnto clere nette lyke atte tyme houre wha baptised penaunce moche horryble hard alle payne wymmen euer suffred trauayllyng delyueryng theyr chyldren also saynt bartylmewe suffryd flayn al quyck saynt stephen stoned stone saynt laurence saynt vyncent brente rosted vpon brennyng cooles al martyrdom tormentes ne ben bayne colde water wytnesse scrypture regarde tormentes purgatorye sowles brenne vntyl purged al theyr synnes lyke golde syluer purged fyned fyre tyl foude purged fyre purgatorye suche nature alle fynde soule dede worde thought hath corned ony synne lytel grete brente purged also ben punysshed purged synnes venyal whyche calle lytel synnes whyche ofte lyke foule thoughtes ydle wordes iapes trufes lye alle vanytees longe tyl soule haue nomore purged clene pure nette worthy sayntefyed entre heuen none may entre yf ryght fyne right clene ryght cleer pthys fyre dreden alle theyr power kepe fro dedely synne kepe holyly theyr body theyr mouth theyr eerys theyr eyen al theyr fyue naturel wyttes fro al synnes also lyuen shold euery day dye come tofore iugement cause none may lyue al wythoute synne lyke sayth salamon seuen tymes day falleth ryghtwysman therfore holy confessyon teerys orysons almesses good dedes ought euery man relyeued put awaye fro synne amende hys lyf iuge hym self hys synnes ende abyde surely last iugement palso lerne knowe euyl flee alle synne grete lytel thenne grete drede god whyche begynnyng alle good good lyf phow ought lyue holyly lerne wel capo lxij ynough leue al synnes euyls lernyd good yf lerne gete vertues may caste put aweye vyces synnes wythoute whyche vertues noo man may lyue wel ne rightfully thenne yf thou wylte lerne lyue wel vertu lerne also deye haue afore sayd deceuere thy spyryte fro thy body thought desyre goo oute world deyeng goo lande lyuyng none shal deye ne neuer wexe olde heuen lerned lyue wel al wysedom alle curtesye may entre vylayne gloryous companye god gloryous virgyne hys moder saynt marye angellys sayntes surhabounde goodes beaultees rychesses honoures strengthe lyghtnes scyence fraunchyse vertues wytte glorye ioye perdurable poynte ypocresye ne trycherye ne losengerye ne dyscorde ne enuye ne hungre ne thryst ne hete ne colde ne euyl ne sorowe ne drede enemyes alway feste ryall espousaylles songe ioye wythoute ende ioye soo grete shal haue tasted one onely drope moost leste ioye shold fyred soo entalented loue god al ioye thys world shold vnto hym stenche tormentes rychesses dunge honour fylthe vyletees desyre come thyder shalle make hym hondred thousand tymes ardatly hate synne loue vertues doo wel loue stronge drede thenne lyf fayr honeste whan persone fleeth al euyls synnes enforceth hym al good may onely fere dampned desyre glorye perdurable loue god grete clennesse vertues haue good lyf whome loue god ledeth moche hastelyer sonner ardantly comen therto lasse costeth serue god drede hare renneth doth grehoud one drede desyre one fleeth chaceth holy man renneth god lyke grehounde hath alwaye eyen desyre heuen seeth praye chaceth forgeteth goodes world lyke gentyl hounde whan seeth praye waye lyf fyue good true louers god gentyl hertes moche louen vertues haten synnes yf certeyn ne shold ne myght knowe synnes ne god shold auenge yet wold deygne ne consente synne al theyr thought payne theyr herte kepe clene f al synnes apparaylle worthy see haue perdurably glorye heuen herte vylaynous entached wyth synne shal neuer entre ne fool ne felonous ne proude man pof iij maner spyrituel goodes capitulo lxiij haue wel shewed one shold lerne deye lede vse good holy lyf gete vertues man knowe wel euydently clennesse synne almesse vertu also one knowe wel certeynlye iuge euyl synne good cone deuyse veray good grete good fro lytel thynge knowen neytherhat ne desyred therfore oughtest thou knowe scryptures sayen somme smale thynges callyd lityl good somme myddel good somme grete good somme veray good ryghtful al world somtyme deceyued gyue grete goodes lytyl grete myddle thys world fayre ben many folysshe marchauntes fooles bye glasse saphyres leed golde bladder lanternes good marchaunte euery thynge knoweth wel clerely trouthe propre vertue lyke holy ghoost enseygneth v another maystre techeth v knowe grete thynges fro smale precyouse fro vyle swete bytter pof goodes fortune capo lxiiij calle smalle goodes goodes fortune whiche dame fortune hath aboute hyr whele alwaye taketh weye gyueth torneth whiche aboue falle vnder ben procyouse stone fooles haue bought rubyes saphyrs emerawdes ben also iewels yonge chyldren god gyueth v solace v wyth drawe loue hym cause knoweth wel ben tendre ble may holde sharpe wayes penaunce anguysshe martyrdom lyke doon good knyghtes god whiche conquere royame heuen strengthe take ttheyr prowesse theyr good vertues thenne grete good ne wel ryghtful yf grete good veray thenne fooles blessyd chyldren god ihesu cryst whyche chosen pouerte shame sharpnesse gyue shewe v ensaumple refused ioyes honoures rychessys thys world yf goodes transytorye worldly temporalle ben veray good thene al veray goodes heuen thenne god parfytelye good happy cause wyl vse suche goodes thenne god good ne naturalle cause gyueth worldly goodes frendes gyueth largely enemyes yf veray good thenne foles al sayntes alle good clerkys wyse phylosophres fledde fro suche worldly goodes despysed dunge yf veray good thenne fayleth holy scrypture calleth lye vanytees nettes grynnes deuyl trewe pater noster ben engynes deuyl whych deceyueth soules thousand maners byndeth taketh holdeth wyse marchaunte wyse man whome holy ghoost enlumyneth veray knowleche oueralle knoweth decerne euery thynge worth seeth ryght wel vnderstondeth world good morsel fylle herte one man therin moche euyl lytel good therfore beholdeth euylles perylles ben therin knoweth wel trouthe comunelye sayd gyueth whyche loueth taketh whiche desyreth suche folke gyuen world haue heuen forsaketh oueral riches ioye fylthe ordure golde leue alle goddes sake rychesses delyces honoures bycome poure world wynne good gete rychesse heuen moost fayrest lyf moste sure may world ben see many maners may one doo prouffyt sauacyon wyth goodes temporelle may haue wythout ouermoche loue god commaundeth man leue al reteyne lytyl preyse vse lytyl loue lyke dyd abraham iob dauyd many eschewed fledde perilles spyrituel prouffyte wyth temporalle goodes wyl bye heuen wyth theyr almesses good dedes bye oute theyr synnes helpe theyr neyghbours loue god drede doubte hym perylles humble self whan see consyder theyr synnes theyr deffaultes whan sharpe streyte weyes penaunce dar goo whan lytel goddes sake wyl suffre gyue whiche moche suffred saue wolde xxxij yere world poure enryche heuen saue wel harde doo lyght thynge leue alle goodes attones reteyne loue pof goodes nature folowe capo lxv moyen myddle goodes ben goodes nature doctryne nature lyke beaulte body prowesse force strengthe vygour lyghtnes debonayrte clere wytte clere engyne fynde good memorye reteyne wel good wy synge wel goodes aforsayd nature bryngeth natyuyte byrthe persone doctryne clergy al goodes goten studye accustomaunce lyke good vertues good maners vertues ben yet veray good ryghtful doo whyche perfytelye good many phylosophre grete clerkys kynges emperours many prynces lordes many goodes dampned helle palso goodes hath lord gyuen enemyes wel frendes sarasyns iewes false crysten men lyke hath good men also thys veray good faylleth nede may loste maulgre hym self though theuys may take robbe yet deth taketh awaye laste also say veray goodes ayden alwaye greuen neuer certeynlye suche goodes suche grace forayn ofte dammage greue haue yf vse wel accordyng god somme auaunte proude despysen whan whome god hath gyuen suche grace suche goodes haue tofore sayd named yf vse wel iustly accordyng god shall gretter tormente helle straytly must acompte yelde rekenynge day dome haue doon haue vsed despended notwythstondyng haue goten goodes god hath lente multeplyeng encrees phere shewed goodes grace capo lxvj haue shortly shewyd lytel good moyen good wyl shewe whyche veray good ryghtful parfyte doeth whyche hath good wyth ryghte vnderstondyng wythoute whyche neuer good wyth ryght good called grace god vertue charytee grace cause gyueth lyf helthe soule wythoute soule deed lyke body dede withoute soule soule deed wythoute grace god called vertue cause adourneth soule good werkys wyth good maners called charyte cause ioyneth soule god also dooth al thynge wyth god charyte thynge ellys dere vnyte perfection beneurte whyche ought entende moche deceyued auncyent phylosophres curyously dysputeden enquyreden souerayn good thys lyf neuer coude fynde ne knowe hit somme sette theyr studye theyr wytte delytes body rychessys honeste grete phylosopher saynt poul whyche rauysshed vnto thyrd heuen passeth alle phylosophres techeth v many reason souerayn good lyf quene vertues loue god haue veray charyte hym self wythoute good ne auaylen alle goodes ryght nought hath thys good charyte hath alle goodes whan al goodes shalle faylle good shal faylle aboue al grete goodes charyte lady thenne grettest good vnder heuen charyte cause thou wylte desyrest thys good whyche ryght called vertue thou desyrest loue moost seche aboue alle goodes wyl yet shewe valure acustomed deuyse thre maners goodes world wyte goodes honourable goodes delectable goodes prouffytable moo goodes ne veray ne good ne fayre thre maners thys seest thou openlye world none desyreth ne loueth ony thynge wene honourable delectable prouffytable pthe proude secheth thynge honourable couetous man secheth thynges prouffytable delycious secheth thynges delectable whan sechen thynge vaynlye euery man ought knowe vert e haue thre propretees vertue moche honourable delectable pro ffytable pwhat vertues ben goodes honourable capo lxvij whyche vertues ben goodes honourable mayst thou see thys manere syxe thynges world moche desyred cause seme moche honourable wete beaulte wytte prowesse power fraunchyse noblesse ben vj fontanyes vanyte vayn glorye cometh sourdeth plante beaulte thynge moche loued thynge moche honourable neuerthelesse beaulte eyen body see loue thynge fals couert vayne false nothynge fayre eyen ben vayn feble see noo thynge skynne wythoutforth thenne myght see clere beest callyd lynx whyche seeth thorugh oute walle shold cl rely see fayr body ny whyte sacke ful stynkyng dunge lyke dunghylle couerd wyth snowe wyth grene grasse palso say thys beaulte moche shorte abydyng sone faylled anone passed fume smoke flour felde medowe anone soule departeth fro body fare wel al beaulte faylled gone thenne beaute body hath soule hath gyuen hym therfore moche fooles al beaulte body gloryfye self beaulte soule ryght beaute whyche alwaye encreaceth neuer shal faylle v ray beaulte whiche soule pleaseth god aungellys seen herte beaulte rendreth gyueth soule grace vertues loue god reformeth reparaylleth rendreth hyr ryght enprynte ymage hyr maker whiche beaulte wythout comparyson best resembleth getyng vertues pluckyng vp caste hym alle synnes kepe hys commaundementes entyerly moost fayre pthenne moost fayre thynge vnder god soule whyche hath parfytely ryght fourme ryght clerete colour flour clerenesse sonne fygure man playsaunce precyous stone al eye body seeth beaulte fylthe foule regarde soule al may thought beaulte may compared soule pof veray sapyence capitulo lxviij wytte clergye thynge moche honourable moche preysed yf thou wylte wyse ryght lerne veray clergye soo thou haue veray good grace vertues veray sapyence enlumyneth herte man lyke sonne enlumyneth alle world wytte passeth surmouteth al wytte world lyke sonne passeth clerenesse mone wytte world ny folye lyke scrypture sayth chyldehode wodenesse folye moche louen world beaulte knowe day fro nyght ne iuge bytwene grete lytel bytwene precyous vyle wene mone sonne wene honour world veray glorye lytel apple grete montayne wene world grete thynge regarde heuen ny pouerte wene glasse saphyr wene theyr strengthe theyr power moche grete whiche feble fraylle glasse palso say chyldehode wytte world moche make wyse kepe ease body delyces whyche lyuen chylde seche nothynge ellys doo theyr propre wylle suche people reason deed therfore lyuen beestys theyr wytte al torned corrupt lyke taste sauour seek man woman grete wyth chylde whyche fyndeth sauour appetyte soure apple brede made whete sauour cool good mete also peple may byleue ioye delyte louyng god serue honoure hym doyng wylle caroyne theyr body ryghtfully iuge betwene swete bytter also say wytte world wodenesse soo moche subtyl fyndyng malyce tengyne deceyue strengthe plee barate ne thynke ne studye sauf auaunce enhaunce self greue thys wytte sayth saynt iames wytte deuyl whiche alwaye payneth hym self harme veray wytte holy ghoost enseygneth techeth frendes lord knowyng wythoute mysprysyng euery thyng worthe sheweth world vayn beyng foule valour louyng sauouryng rychessys ben vyle transytorye delytes bytter gyueth feelyng loue god vertues thynge veray precyous swete veray fylleth hert nouryssheth susteyneth precyous one may bye god al hath swete manna al thynges maketh swete labour sorowe wepynges shame trybulacyons aduersytees martyrdom al paynes al one may thynke loue maketh sauour lyke su wytte sapyence wherof scrypture sayth thys sapyence oute whyche groweth purete veray conscyence pof prowesse knyghtes ihesu cryst capo lxix say vertues charyte gyuen veray prowesse thenne prowesse right knyghtes god whyche holy ghoost adoubeth armeth wyth vertues charyte prowesse thre partyes hardynesse strengthe stedfastnes none noble ryght yf haue thre thynges yf hardy prudent entreprenaut grete thynges stronge puyssant pursiewe ferme stable fynysshe wythoute wytte wythout purueaunce nothyng auayllen none iij thynges lyke sayth book arte chyualrye errour wythoute bataylle may amended anone compared folyssh enterpryse lyeth lytel prouffyte moche despence grete payn perylle thenterpryses called wyse hardy world theyr bodyes theyr soules putten synne perylle payne gete lytel loo preysyng whiche moche vayne lytel endureth p vertue maketh man grete herte wyse enterpryse whan maketh man whiche nothyng erthe soo hardy dare enterpryse conquere royalme heuen vaynquysshe alle deuylles helle stronge pthys enterprise good wyse moche prouffytable therin lytel perylle lytel payne glorye honour prouffyte inestymable perdurable wythout mesure hath noo vertu hath grete herte lyke hym aferde nought suche ben doubten euylles aduersytees perylles trybulacyons world haue drede lese whyche may longe kepe p haue noo grete hert gyue hit ouer nought lyke doon gyue theyr hertes loue goodes fortune trouthe ryght nought fylthe charge ordure regarde goodes glorye perdurable p thenne suche people lyke chylde loueth better apple myrrour royame vertu gyueth grete herte ryght vertue maketh conquere heuen despyse world bere grete dedes penaunce supporte gladly suffre al euylles world endure goddes sake also wythstonde resyste alle assaultes deuyl lyke wyse prudente seneke saith wepynges myschauces sorows trybulacons harmes shame perylles al whyche euyl fortune may menace doo haue nomore power ayenst vertu one drope water shold see vertu maketh man hardy lyon stronge holyfaunte ferme durable sone whyche alwaye renneth neuer wery thenne prowesse ne strengthe vertues pof veray seygnorye gyueth grace vertues lxx thus none veray seygnorye vertues grete lord knoweth alle world suche lord gyueth man suche vertues grace setteth man ryght estate whiche fyrst sette made man made suche honour suche seygnorye lord ouer al creature vnder heuen whome al thynges obeyed whome noo thynge myght noye ne greue ryght estate man seygnorye lost seygnorye synne myght recouer ageyn vertu vertue setteth man hyghe setteth world vnder foot maketh hym conuerse heuen vertue maketh man good ryght gretter lord world kyng royame goodes world hath moche herte desyreth hath vsage sustenaunce moche may haue suffysaunce suffysantlye kyng hath royame al good hath euyl al therfore alle dooth hys prouffyte preyseth god thanketh loueth hym doubteth serueth thys seeth knoweth euery creature made serue hym also another seygnorye moche grete withoute whome none ryzt lord emperour lord hym self body hert whiche iustyceth holdeth good pee dooth wylle herte ioyned wylle god al god doeth thanketh hym playseth hym wel thys seygnorye vertu gyueth hym hath thys speketh seneke sayth grete honour gyueth god whan thou art lord emperour thy self tha kyng ha lord god many kynges emperours grete lordes haue ben world also baron haue citees castellis royames haue seygnorye lordes theyr hertes cause tormenteth ofte wrath maletalente couetyse desyre may accomplysshe phere spoken veray fraunchyse capo lxxj thys say none hath veray frau chyse yf haue grace vertue thenne yf thou wylte knowe veray frauchyse man woman right thou oughtest vnderstonde man hath iij maner fraunchyses one nature another grace thyrd glorye fyrst free wylle whiche man may chese frely good euyl fraunchyse holdeth euery man god frely man may wronge ne alle deuylles helle may enforce man ayenste hys wylle synne wythout accorde consentemente yf man dyd euyl ayenst wylle shold haue therof synne moche wyse myght eschewe lyke sayth saynt austyn fredom fraunchyse hath euery man fredom chyldren ne wood men ne fooles cause haue vsage reason whiche chese good euyl man putteth awaye hym thys fraunchyse grete partye whan synneth dedelye selleth hym self vnto deuyll delyte hys synne yeldeth hym selfe vnto hym bycometh seruaunt synne may caste hym self ne put hym fro wylle hath deserued deth helle yf grace god helpe hym second fraunchyse suche wyse man hath world whome god hath frauchysed grace vertues seruyce deuyl fro synne bonde golde ne syluer ne temporalle goodes world ne theyr bodyes whyche caroyn ne goodes fortune whyche deth may sone take awaye haue theyr hertes lyfte vp gyuen god preyse thyng goodes world ne honour ne vanytees ne kyng ne duc ne meschaunce ne pouerte ne shame ne deth deed world haue hert deceueryd taken awaye fro loue world desyre deth lyke werkman payment iourney dayes labour labourer hyre also lyke ben tormet fortune see desyre come port salue lyke prysonner desyreth good delyueraunce pylgrym desyreth come ageyn hys contreye yf parfytelye free thys world lyke creature may thenne fere ne doubte thynge god greet pee herte haue thenne theyr herte god heuen desyre thys fraunchyse cometh grace vertue yet al fraunchyse ny seruytude regarde thyrd fraunchyse haue glorye verayly free verayly delyuerd fro alle perylles fro alle tormentes fro fere deth deth fro grynnes empesshemes world fro myserye fro pouerte fro al payne herte body wythoute retornyng whiche thynge none free thys world parfyte pof veray noblesse capo lxxij shal haue second fraunchyse whyche haue spoken shal come grete noblesse veray noblesse cometh gentyl hert certeyn none hert gentyl yf loue god noblesse serue loue god kepe hym fro al synnes seruage deuyl ne vylanye angre god synne ther man ryght gentyl ne noble gentylnesse hys body touchyng body ben al sonnes one moder erthe fylthe whyche al haue taken flesshe blood parte none gentyl ne free swete fader ihesu cryst whiche kyng heuen fourmed body erthe created soule ymage semblauce al lyke wyse carnal fader moche glad ioyous whan hys sone resembleth hym ryght fader ihesu cryst holy scrypture hys messagers techeth v shold payne self resemble hym therfore sent v hys blessyd sone ihesu cryst therthe brynge gyue v veray exemplayre whyche may reformed hys ymage semblaunce lyke dwelle hye cytee heuen angellys sayntes heuen eueryche moche hye noble proprely bereth thys fayre ymage therfore holy men thys world payne self knowe god loue hym wyth alle theyr hert purge clense kepe alle synnes moche herte creature pure clene wythout synne moche seeth clerely euydently precious face ihesu cryst soo moche loueth ardauntly moche resembleth proprelye hath gretter glorye thys veray noblesse god hath gyuen v pand therfore sayth ryght wel saynt iohan appostle euangelyst thenne shal sone god shal resemble hym proprely wha shal see hym euydently lyke shal glorye whan shal heuen man seeth dyscouerd ne clerely beaute god lyke sayth saynt poule thenne shal see hym face face proprely clerely whan shal glorye ioyous companye p veray noblesse man thenne begynneth grace vertues parfyght glorye noblesse maketh holy ghoost hertes purgeth culumyneth trouthe parfyte charyte grettest goodes god hath done aungellis lyke saynt denys sayth whiche resemble theyr maker thus werketh holy ghoost grace vertue hertes good men whyche reformed thymage semblaunce theyr maker ihesu cryst moche may mortal lyf reyse self soo god enbrace self soo wyth loue god al theyr entendement al theyr entencyon theyr wylle theyr memorye alle conuerted god loue enbracement desyre whyche encreaceth ioyneth vnyeth herte god may thynge wylle god wylle bytwene god one self wylle thenne hath thymage semblaunce god moche may thys world moost grete noblesse moost hye gentylnesse whyche one may atteyne mounte pha good god ferre thys noblesse fro thys hyenesse ben make noble soo queynt thys poure noblesse haue theyr moder erthe whyche bereth nouryssheth hogges wel dooth emperours kynges auaute gentylnesse cause wene gentyl fylthe thys kynrede parage conne ryght wel recounte telle syde noblesse beholde noo thynge alle whyche cometh veray noblesse gentyl parage shold beholde take hede theyr veray exemplayr ihesu cryst whyche loued honoured moder dyd ony man neuerthelesse whan one sayd ihesu cryst syr moder cosyns stonden wythoute seche answerd sayd moder fader cosyns someuer wylle fader heuen broder fader suster moder thys noble syde gentyl kynrede whyche cometh groweth herte veray glory groweth vayne noblesse pryde phow charyte grettest vertues capo lxxiij haue suffysauntly shewyd ther ben goodes honourable ryght vertues charyte fayr loue god none good prouffytable without vertu charyte wytnesseth v saynt poul sayth thus yf haue moche scyence knewe al clergye al langages spake wel men angellys knewe al scryptures counseylles god yf delyuerd body martyrdom gaf al poure peple yf dyd myracles montaygnes lepen one place another yf vertu charyte alle thys shold auaylle pnow beholde thenne take hede saynt poul ought byleue hath named grettest thynges good one may doo moost auaylle prouffyten penaunces body suffre martyrdom ayde poure peple conuert synners haue scyence langages thappostle sayth al thynges auayllen wythoute charyte yf suche grete goodes auayllen shold lasse god auaylle mayst thou knowe reason
