hym god soo strongelye nothyng may dysseuere ne desioyne hym thenne wylle thou say thys word thy name sayntyfyed v say gyue v yefte sapyence whyche may soo fyned golde syluer fornays clensed fro alle ordure synne dronken loue al loues v bytter whyche soo gyuen thy seruyce neuer retche none charge thende onelye wesshen fro alle synnes dyed grayne renewed rebaptysed precyous blode ihesu cryst deuocyon feruent loue thys blessyd name good fader ihesu cryst soo confermed v good fader good sone seruauntes obedyent alle hys commandements suche manere thyng someuer may come ne happene desioyne thys fastnes ne thys grace moche grete grace god wha wylle creature humayn rooted god confermed may wagge ne moeue temptacyon moche gretter thynge whan one affermed loue god dronken swetenesse soulas ne comforte ne playsaunce may hym thenne herte parfytelye confermed god whan memorye fastned ioyned hym may thynke noo thynge hym thys requyre whan saye sanctificetur nomen tuum say syr thy name sayntyfyed v phere second petycyon requeste holy pater noster capitulo lxxx aduemat regnum tuu second petycyon requeste holy pater noster praye requyre royame god come v wythin v lord sayth gospel dyscyples royalme god wythin vnderstonde wel may whan god gyueth persone herte spyrite vnderstondyng thus sonne taketh awaye derknesses nyght wasteth cloudes mystes mornyng ryght soo wasteth thys spyrite taketh awaye alle derknesses herte sheweth hym al synnes defaultes grete smale lyke rayes sonne sheweth mote duste hous p also spyrite vnderstondynge sheweth parte onelye within hym vnder hym helle whyche aboue hym heuen whyche aboute hym alle fayre creature whych al preysen god wytnessen god fayr good wyse puyssant swete grete seeth moost clere creature moost desyryng see god lete hym consydere pure ne worthy see hym thenne good herte trewe deuoute chauffeth hym angry wyth hym self thenne begynneth entre herte examyne hym fyndeth many synnes vyces pouertees deffaultes troublynges herte thoughtes euyl wylle angry wyth hym self grete contrycyon desplayser hath hys synnes thenne begynneth clense herte purge hym al ordure synne bytter repentaunce deuoute confessyon sharpe condygne penaunce whan hath longe ledde thys lyf hath caste oute al hys synnes veray confessyon thenne fyndeth pee reste consolacion tereth soo moche god falle ageyn synne hym semeth alle world hym helle regarde thys clerenesse thys pee fyndeth hys herte thys demaunde god whan saye aduemat regnum tuum saye fayr fader plese holy ghoost wyl enlumyne v hert clense purge fro al synnes vouchesauf come dwelle kyng lord gouernour commaundour oure hertes al herte hys kyng lorde alwaye may see hym lyf perdurable haue royame god within v therfore sayth lord gospel royame god tresour hyd felde herte good man whiche grete alle world pthe iij peticion requeste holy pater noster lxxxj fiat voluntas tua sicut celo terra iij peticion requeste praye lord wylle doon v lyke done heuen holy angellys whyche ben heuen whiche ben enlumyned confermed god may wylle none thyng god wyl may haue peticion ne thys perfection haue yefte counceyl whyche thyrd yefte holy ghoost whych techeth v good wylle conuerte caytyf fraylle wylle v growe noo propre wylle wylle onely lady al herte hooly v someuer wylle lyke wylle doon holy aungellys heuen whyche may synne alwaye done wylle god wythoute mespryse gaynsayeng p hast thou herde thre petycyons fyrst requestes holy pater noster whyche ben hyest moost worthy fyrst demaunde yefte sapyence second yefte vnderstondyng thyrd yefte counceyl lyke haue tofore shewed iij thynges requyre cause shold haue thys mortal lyf parfytelye shewe vnto good fader ihesu cryst desyres alwaye heuen ought ende thre requestes petycyons doon accomplisshed v lyf perdurable demaude presente lyf pin four petycyons comen speke another langage say good fader ihesu cryst gyue v pardone v kepe v delyuer v yf haue ihesu crist foure petycyons requestes thys presente world ben deed necessary euery persone thys mortal lyf pthe iiij petycyon requeste capitulo lxxxij panem nostrum cotidianum da nobis hodie wel techeth v good mayster ihesu crist speke humbly wysely techeth v say fayr fader gyue v thys day brede cotydyan dayly may sone lasse demaunde fader onelye brede passe forth day demaundeth none oultrage ne wyne ne flesshe ne fysshe demaundeth brede nomore yere ne yet weke passe wyth day onelye thys semeth lytel thynge demaunde certaynly requyre moche grete thynge whan requyre abbot brede abbay requyre fraternyte companye parte right al goodes abbey ryght hym demaundeth god thys dayly breed hath fraternyte parte companye ryght alle goodes ben heuen thys blessyd brede heuen blessyd couente brede heuen brede angellys brede delectable brede lyf perdurable gyueth lyf vnderstondyng neuer deye preserueth man wherof god sayth gospel brede lyf whyche descended fro heuen shal ete brede shal alway lyue wythoute deyeng thys breed ryght good mete hyt stauncheth alle hongres world fylleth man replenyssheth thys dooth mete breed mete thou takest sacrament aulter mete thou oughtest take grete ardour grete deuocyon hert grete desyre vnderstonde thou ouztest byleue feythfully thys mete moche precyous veray body ihesu cryst soule godhede al togyder wythout errour wythoute demaunde aske ony ferther god may man may vnderstonde man ouzt vnderstonde chewe precyous mete lyke oxe fedeth grasse cheweth cudde thenne taketh say one ought remembre deuoutlye ofte partyes bountees grace lord al sorowes ihesus cryste suffred erthe v thenne hert fyndeth sauour thys precyous mete causeth ryght grete ardour loue god ryght grete desyre wylle suffre al may hym may al thys dooth vertu blessyd brede sacramente masse whiche veray precyous b ihesu cryst thys brede comforteth orceth herte wel stronge suffre gr te thynges loue god thys may yf haue fourth yefte holy ghoost whyche yefte strengthe whyche armeth encorageth nyght god maketh hym ne gladly martyrd suffre ioyously tormentes mayst thou see whan demaunde brede angellys demaude yefte strengthe lyke bodyly brede materyal susteyne body enforce ryght yefte strengthe maketh herte stronge suffre grete thynges god brede celestial angellis calle made paste sone god fader sone borne gloryous vyrgyn marye blessyd gloryous vyrgyn fro whome came blessyd floure debonayr ihesus whyche fryed crucyfyed crosse redeme world fro paynes helle thys dyd grete brennyng loue vnto v bysquyt whyche garnysshed hys shyppe holy chyrche passe grete see thys perillous worlde oures lefte v hys departyng leue takyng laste testamente swete ihesu cryst right large moost grete moost ryche tresour myght leue v gaf hym self v moost fayrest iewel myght gyue v ought deuoutelye clenly reuerently kepe hym wythout synne thys brede angellys ought euery day vse loue hym mynde holy passyon verayly oures noo thynge may take awaye fro v ayenst wylle oures hym self calle brede cotydyan saye euery day vnderstonde cotydyan distribucyon gyueth hys preestys relygyous peple euery day whyche doon seruyses synge hys mass hys houres alle good crysten men wymmen euery day veray loue deuoutely make remembraunce dolorous passyon ihesu cryst suffred v pthe groos prouende brede aungellys take haruest heuen whan shal see swete ihesu cryst dyscouerd hys ryght grete beaulte lyke therfore sayd cotydyan euery day v necessarye euery one ought take holy sacrament aulter lyke doon preestys whiche ben therto ordeyned p otherwyse euery good crysten man woman ought take hym ryght fayth thys brede ryght precyous ryght noble ryght wel arayed thys mete ryal whyche alle maner delyces al good sauours lyke sayth book sapyence none erthely mete ought gyuen raskayll hertes gentyl noble whiche ben purged clensed fro al ordure synne veray repentaunce deuoute confessyon entyer satysfactyon penaunce p vertu brede angellys saith saynt mathew theuangelyst calleth brede sursubstancyal say passeth surmounteth alle substaunce alle creature praysyng vertue alle dygnytees maners valure none may better name ne descryue ne suffysauntlye calle hit breed sursubstancyal p sayd mete substancyous whan therin ynough substaunce nourysshyng soo moche nourysshyng soo moche sayd substancyall pand cause thys precyous breed aungellys nourysshyng vertue good euer may thought sayd sayd onelye hyt substancyous bytwene ony vnderstondyng supposyng sayd sursubstancious brede requyre good fader ihesu cryste praye hym wyl gyue v day preset mortal lyf thede may make good iourneye abyde gladly rewarde ende lyf glorye perdurable phere foloweth v petycion request holy pater noster capitulo lxxxiij dimitte nobis debita nostra sicut no dimittimus debitoribus nostris request petycyon requyre demaunde good fader heuen wyl pardonne foryeue v synnes trespaces lyke foryeue haue trespaced v trespasse v thene say thus fayr fader quyte v debtes lyke quyte dettours dettes ben synnes whyche haue encreased vpon soules best moost dere wedde may fyne wherof synnar one dedely synne whiche soo sone passed delyte touchyng dede bounden grete vsure hath noo power paye ne fynyssbe payne helle whyche wythoute ende p oweth vnto god whome hath dysplesed grete amendes hath noo power paye alle lyf yf lyued hondred yere myght ne coude make suffysaut penaunce one dedely synne onely yf god wold vse hys ryghtful iustyce shold neuer fogyuen pand therfore byhoueth bytter grete repentaunce wycked synnar retorne vnto mercy debonayr blessyd lord ihesu cryste crye hym mercy demaunde pardon foryeuenes p ryght courte iustyce synner shal iuged condeuipned vnto deth perdurable therfore good fader ihesu cryst softe debonayr foryeue pardone large curtoys yeue praye hym wyl pardone foryeue v synnes trespaces thynke consider wel thou prayest thou sayst pardone v synnes trespaces lyke pardone v haue trespaced god shal foryeue ne pardone v hym self sayth gospel yf foryeue pardone haue trespaced v thenne saith pater noster yf kepe hert rancour felonnye prayeth ayenst hym self hym self prayeth god forgyue hym synnes whan sayth foryeue lyke forgyue therfore al tymes thou shalt say thy pater noster tofore god seeth thyn hert thou oughtest forgyue al euyl talentes cast thyn hert al ire alle rancour otherwyse thy prayer ayenst yf seme hard thynge greuous foryeue pardone hate wylle euyl haue moche trespaced myssayed thynke god pardoned deth crucefyed hym gyue exaumple forgyue yet praye haue trespaced god forgyue yet wel good helpe yf haue nede sayth gospel grete thynge ne grete meryte ayenst god good v good ne loue loue v done paynyms sarasyns iewes synners pbut chyldren god fayth grace named crysten blessyd lord ihesu cryste heyres wyth hym herytage heuen ought foryeue eche also ought loue enemyes saye theyr persones praye theym good yf haue nede comandeth god gospel thenne ought onely hate synnes loue soules lyke membres one body loue supporte eche yf one membre hurte aduenture aduengeth hym therfore ben al one body ihesu cryste lyke thappostle sayth ought loue supporte eche hate ne greue dooth otherwyse homycyde hym self thys sayth scrypture suche say pater noster better auaylable coude say aryght pardoneth ne foryeueth wyth hert wyth mouthe moeueth iuge ayenst hym prayer make god requyre hym yefte scyence whyche maketh man wyse cunnyng spyrite sheweth hym fro whes cometh whyther gooth hath hath trespaced moche hath lente moche oweth whan seeth hath wherof paye thenne spyryte maketh hym repente wepe syghe crye god mercy say good lord foryeue pardonne debtes synnes moche endetted vnto euylles synnes haue commysed doon good dedes haue forgoten lefte whiche ought myght haue doon goodes benefaytes thou hast done grete bountees haue al day receyued euyl vsed haue euyl seruyd cause lord moche drede doubte make payement requyre pardone whiche owe vnto whan thys spyryte scyence hath thus enlumyned hym knoweth defaultes synnes thenne casteth oute hert alle hate rancour pardoneth alle euyl wylle angre yf haue ony yf haue ony wylle purpose pardone foryeue wyth good hert yf ony haue trespaced hym thenne may wel say fayr fader forgyue v trespaces lyke haue trespaced v pthe vj peticion request pater noster capo lxxxiiij et ne no inducas temptacionem brent chylde fyre dredeth somtyme fallen synne whan hys synne pardoned hym doubtous aferde hath drede temptacyon synne tofore therfore prayeth god whome hath moche trespaced also hath forgyuen pardoned hym wyl kepe hym fro fallyng hit ageyn saith thus et ne no inducas temptacionem saye fayr swete fader suffre thou entre temptacyon consente ony synne deuyl temptour synne crafte serueth hous god preue newe knyghtes god yf temptacyon good prouffytable good peple god whyche dooth al thynge prouffyte wolde neuer suffre temptacyon shold come saynt bernard sayth whan temptour smyteth v backe forgeth v crownes glorye lyke smyteth backe good knyght forgeth hym praysyng hys glorye deuyl tempteth man proprely thende take hym aweye departe hym holly loue lord ihesu cryste ptherfore prayed prayeth v saynt poule appostle vnto hys dyssyples founded terme toure roted tree charyte loue god soo temptacyon may moeue theym ne make stakre ne quaure pand therfore thys petycyon request requyre demaunde ayde helpe god bataylle ayenst fende wyl gyue v yefte pyte grace arouseth bedeweth hert maketh hym swete pyetous maketh hym al rendre wexe grene bere fruyt ynough good werkes wythoutforth wythinforth wythin make stedfast ferme rootes londe lyuyng peple pthat lyke good cyment whyche maad walles sarazynoys whyche may broken ne defeated wyth pykoys ne wyth hamer whan say thenne et ne no inducas temptacionem say swete fader make hertes ferme stable moeue ne quauer noo temptacion come grace yefte pyte praye noo wyse tempted folysshe prayer shameful lyke sone lord another noble man shold adoubed newe knyght shold say fader fayr fader praye ye deporte forbere kepe neuer see batayl ne tournoye pwe ought wel wylle tempted grete prouffyte many maners humble doubcous wyse many caases bettyr proued hardy salamon sayth hath tempted may knowe thynge ryght lyke one knoweth batayl troye sayeng may know hym self ne infirmyte ne strengthe enemyes ne subtylte ne god trewe nede ayde frende ne many tymes hath kepte v many perylles synnes al reason shal cone loue god aryght ne thake hym hys yeftes yf tempted praye hym kepe v hertes entre resyste fyght vaynquysshe fende enemye whan consente synne p seuenth petycyon pater noster capo lxxxv ed libera no malo amen saynt austyn sayth al temptacyons ben v eyther wel leue wel yeftes good man pater noster ben sette forthe ordre theyr dygnyte hye tofore lower p callyd yeftes thre reason capo lxxxvij svche maner grace haue name yeftes iij thynges thre reason fyrst theyr dygnyte valour yf man court kyng gyue robe chylde pour man dysshe weyght thynge ought called yefte kynge therfore calleth saynt iames thappostle al temporel goodes god gyueth yefte lytel yeftes whych ben moeuable passyng reprysyng reprehendyng whan al yeftes shal faylle vij yeftes shal abyde alwaye theyr ferme estate thenne soo proprely oures may lese ageyn wylle lyke may lese pthe thyrd reason pryncypal selue yeftes gyuen purely loue thou knowest wel yefte leseth name yefte whan gyuen purely loue whan yeuer yeueth ony yefte owne prouffyte yefte marchandyse whan beholdeth bounte receyued seruyse yefte bounte yeftes holy ghoost yeftes fader sonne al theyr werkys yeftes ben comyn purpoos ben two reason one lyke werkes puyssaunce myght ben appropred god fader werkes sapyence god sone ryght soo ben werkys grace bounte appropred holy ghoost bountees ben lyke sayth saynt denys spende gyue hym self yf man yeue whyche coste hym nought grete bounte cause holy ghoost seuen yeftes expendeth gyueth hym self hertes lyke sayth saynt poule lyke seuen stremes therfore ben callyd proprely yeftes holy ghoost fontayn ben stremes pthat cause holy ghoost proprely loue bytwene fader sonne cause loue propre fyrst pryncypal yefte man may yeue thenne wyth ryght yefte ben gyuen al wythoute thys yefte none called yefte truly ne ryghtfully therfore holy ghoost yefte yeuar gyueth hym self yeuen eueryche seuen yeftes whyche gyueth conferme loue vnto feruent fyne veray clene pwhy vij yeftes moo ne lasse capo lxxxix two thynges man saued fro flee euyl good hate flee euyl causeth v yefte drede vj yeftes cause v good yefte drede vssher grete masse saye grete menasse sentence god paynes helle whiche alwaye redy apparaylled ayenst synuars watche castel neuer slepeth thys wedar gardyn wedeth plucketh vp al euyl herbys tresourer kepeth hert alle goodes ben therin vj yeftes make v al good dedes oughtest thou know lyke clerenes sonne thou seest thyn eyen yeueth clerenes world vertu enuygoure strengthe al myddle thyrd lowe moost hye ben lyke ben kynges couceyl alwaye wyth god nerre hym see hym hym secretes moyen myddle ben baron bayllyes gouerne loue kepen al royam gone comen lerne couceyl whiche comande make done lowest ben lyke seruauntes offycers whiche haue theyr craftes done offyces message sayd maner ensaumple ben iij estate chyldren god erth whyche holy ghoost ledeth conduyteth sayth saynt poul one estate hat ben world lyuen commandementes god holy chyrche byleue theyr prelate estate ben parfyte al haue theyr hert world mortal lyf haue theyr conuersacyon heuen theyr body erthe theyr herte wyth god thyrd ben myddle estate whyche gouerne self wel lyuen counceyl gospel onelye commandements thre maner people techeth holy ghoost ledeth gouerneth vj yeftes departeth grace eueryche benygne volente wylle sayth thappostle two fyrst vj yeftes apperteyne ben fyrst estate yefte scyence techeth yefte pyte maketh werke ij myddle apperteyne moyen estate yefte counceyl gouerneth yefte strengthe accomplyssheth werkes ij last apperteyne moost hye estate yefte vnderstondyng enlumyneth yefte sapyence confermeth ioyneth wyth god another reason wherfore ben vij yeftes holy ghoost seuen yeftes wedeth plucketh taketh awaye vij synnes vyces fro hertes persones planteth nouryssheth vij vertues contrarye make perfytely man honoured ben goodes holy ghoost maketh hertes descendeth seuen yeftes tofore descende vnto vertues whiche ben contrarye seuen dedely synnes wyl shortly speke seuen vertues whyche thre ben callyd dyuyne four callyd foure cardynal vertues pof seuen vertues whome thre dyuyne foure cardynal capitulo lxxxx thre fyrst vertues dyuyne saynt poul thappostle calleth fayth hope charyte callyd dyuyne cause godly ordeyne herte god fayth lyke saynt austyn sayth setteth v vnder god maketh v knowe hym knowleche hym lord whome holde al whyche haue good hope sayth enhaunceth v god maketh v stronge hardy entrepryse loue god whiche passeth vertu strengthe man charyte sayth saynt austyn ioyneth v god charyte none thynge chyere vnyte dere onehede maketh hert god alle one sayth saynt poul fayth byholdeth god souerayn vnyte hope beholdeth god souerayn hyenesse charyte souerayn bounte iij vertues ben deuyded iij degree loue iij thynges loued one cause one hath herde hereth grete good hym cause hath receyued grete good hym cause entendeth haue grete good hym iij maners loue ben iij vertues loue fayth hereth werketh loue hope feleth sauour requyreth loue charyte taketh seeth tasteth holdeth p foure cardynal vertues whyche man ought gouerne hym capitulo lxxxxj four cardynal vertues speken moche auncyent phylosophres holy ghoost gyueth enseygneth better hondred tymes sayth salamon book sapyence fyrst iiij vertues prudence second attemperaunce iij strengthe fourth iustyce iiij vertues ben callyd cardynallys cause ben moost pryncypal emonge vertues whyche auncyent phylosophres speken iiij vertues man gouerneth hym self world lyke pope gouerneth al holy chyrche hys cardynalles p prudence kepeth man deceyued none engyne enemye attemperaunce kepeth man corrupt none euyl loue strengthe kepeth hym vaynquysshed ne ouercome wrath drede sorowe holdeth man good estate toward hym self iustyce setteth man ryght ordre ryght estate anenst hym self iustyce rendreth eche man whiche ben iiij toures iiij corner hous good man maketh stronge sure good prudence garnyssheth toward eest pourueaunce perylles attemperaunce garnyssheth toward south ayenst euyl heetys strengthe garnyssheth toward north euyll coldes iustyce garnyssheth toward west ayenst euyl raynes yet ageyn four cardynal vertues foloweth lxxxxij iiij vertues haue dyuers offyces moche dyuers theyr werkys lyke sayth aucyent phylosophre named plato book made foure vertues deuydeth moche subtylly sayth prudence hath iij offyces vertu al man doth sayth thynketh ordeyned al ledde lyne rule reason al werkys pourueyeth vse thordynaunce god al seeth iugeth grete lord shold semeth shold haue onely vertu thre thynges shold gouerne hym p vertu attemperaunce capitulo lxxxxiij vertu attemperaunce hath iij offyces hert hath vertu wylle ne coueyteth thynge whyche ought repente thynges breketh lawe dysmesurably putteth hym self alwaye vnder yoke reason thynge doubteth alle couetyses world say hath vertu kepeth hym corrupt thre thynges foulen shaman world pof vertu strengthe capitulo lxxxxiiij vertu strengthe hath also iij offyces man hath vertu hert lyft hym self vpon hye aboue perylles world thynge doubteth sauf vylonye synne bereth aduersyte prosperyte suffreth withoute bowe ryght syde ne lyfte syde moche good shold knyght god thre thynges shold wel proued iij vertues armen ordeyne adourne man touchyng thre partes hert whiche ben callyd reason loue vygour prudence kepeth reason deceyued attemperaunce kepeth loue corrupt strengthe kepeth vygour myght ouercome pof vertu iustyce capitulo lxxxxv ivstyce maketh man lyue ordynatly emonge lyke plato sayth phylosophre vertu maketh man doth vnto euery man whiche oweth rendreth reuerence honour aboue hym frendshyp pee concorde ben lyke hym grace pyte ben vnder hym iiij vertues sayth sayd phylosophre man thenne worthy gouernour hym self iiij vertues studyed auncyen phylosophres despyseden al world tacquyre gete vertu wysedom therfor callyd phylosophres moche say loue sapyence po good god shold confounde v make v aferd paynyms without lawe wryton nothynge knewe grace god ne yeftes holy ghoost neuertheles styed vp montayn perfection lyuyng force propre vertu daygned take hede world ne euyl ne consent synne ben cristen men haue veray fayth knowe commandements god haue grace holy ghoost yf wyll synnes cause may prouffite helth anenst god day myght yere defoule self lye bynethe swyne myre ordure world synne fylthe donge delyces world therfore sayth saynt poule paynym without lawe shal iuge v atte day iugement haue lawe neyther holde ne kepe cause ryzt fayth ne grace holy ghoost ne vertu ne quycke ne fayth may wel know vertues good fayr moche dyfference bytwene brennyng cole dede cole lyuyng man dede man moche dyfference bytwene vertu wythout charyte vertu wyth charyte whiche boute valure lyf vertues wherof saynt austyn sayth whan speketh iiij vertues deuydeth iiij maner loues iiij thynges veray loue doth sayth vertu prudence loue hert whyche veryly wysely refuseth al whiche may greue ennoye hym cheseth al whyche may aydeto haue whiche loueth god vertu attemperauce loue hert whiche gyueth hym self entyerly wythout corruptyon whyche loueth god vertue strengthe loue herte whyche man serueth onely whyche loueth god hym setteth man al thynges vnder fote despyseth thenne vertu iustyce setteth man right estate aboue al thynges vnder god without iiij vertues none may mounte montayn perfectyon wyl mounte hye hym byhoneth alther fyrst haue prudence whiche maketh man despyse world haue hit vertu strengthe whiche gyueth hym grete hert stronge stable courage enpryse pursiewe grete thynges partye haue vertu attemperaunce cause ouer charged ne euyl caryed haue hym vertu iustyce may lede hym ryght path good iuste waye wythout synne shewe hym holy werkys oweth conquere royame heuen lyke god dyd iacob sayth book sapyence thus may haue iiij vertues shal wel parfyte blessyd world shal pee hert ioye spyrytuel thynge shal faylle hym shal haboude grace god shal haue hym whome shal delyte p foloweth man may take aweye put hym vij dedely synnes gete vertues lxxxxvj late v come ageyn mater pray al hert holy ghoost wyl inspyre enseygne hertes aduocate teche v shewe vij yeftes holy ghoost plucke take aweye seuen dedely synnes fro hertes therin wylle vouchesauf plante seuen vertues yefte holy drede whych maketh iust lxxxxvij yefte drede fyrst yeftes casteth oute hert al synnes lyke haue sayd tofore proprely yefte drede plucketh oute taketh awaye destroyeth rote pryde planteth place plante humylyte beholde vnderstonde wel synnar holdeth hym slepeth synne lyke rybaulde slepeth dronke hath al lost atte tauerne al naked poure hath thynge feleth thynge ne complayneth weneth moche grete lord whan hath slepte cometh ageyn hym self oute hys dronkennesse thenne feleth harme knoweth folye complayneth losse domage fyrst good holy ghoost doth synnar whan vysyteth hym gyueth hym ageyn wytte mynde bryngeth hym ageyn knowe hym self aduertyseth seeth goodes hath loste pouerte perylle hath hys synne lyke dyd sone good man whiche wasted dyspended hys herytage dyssolucyon rybauldrye suche confusyon myserye became hym byhoued kepe swyne fede lyue theyr releef mete lyke lord ihesu cryst sheweth v exaumple gospel yet also synnar sayth salamon lyke hym slepeth myddle see grete perylle tormente feleth noo thynge ne hath fere therof whan holy ghoost awaketh hym felyth seeth perylle begynneth haue drede hym self pyet also synnar lyke hym pryson feteryd yrons boltes hath many kepars lyke saynt peter prysone kyng herode caytyf synnar thynketh thynge prouoste ne iustyce ne galowes tarye hym slepeth dremeth goeth weddyng feste grace holy ghoost lyke aungel awoke saynt peter delyuerd hym fro hande kyng herode grace holy ghoost awaketh synnar delyuerth hym hande fro puyssaunce deuyl helle yet also synnar lyke hym weneth stronge hole hath dethe vnder teeth hath humour euyl corrupte wythin body thenne dyeth within moneth wende haue lyued xl yere lyke sayth elyuans verse speken deth sayen thus go ye awaye ye whystelars gapars suche couerd vnder theyr clothes wene hole fatte shalle lyue vnto marche p holy ghoost lyke vnto good physycyen sheweth hym maladye sekenesse moeueth fro hym humour gyueth vnto hym bytter drynke whyche heleth hym rendreth hym lyf ryght soo troubleth lord synnar bytter contrycyo wha helyth hym fro synnes bytter drynke lyke sayth prophete psaulter fereth hym bryngeth hym ageyn knowe hym self lyke dyd adam fyrst fader whan hydde hym emonge tree paradys terrestre thenne sayd god hym adam art thou thre demaudes made god angel cha bryer holy abraham whyche named agar whan fledde fro hyr lady aungel sayd agar fro whens comest thou whyther goest thou doost thou iij demaundes maketh holy ghoost synnar whan awaketh hym hys synnes aslepe reyseth hym openeth hym eyen hert gyueth hym ageyn wytte mynde art thou sayth say beholde caytyf sorowe peryll thou art world thou art lyke hym peryssheth see slepyng shyppe ne feleth ne vnderstondeth ne apperceyueth perylle say caytyf beholde ageyn thy lyf fro bacward thou comest fro tauerne deuyl thou hast wasted thy lyf loste thy tyme al goodes god hath gyuen doste thou say consyder thou art faynt frayl wery slowe toward thy body toward thy soule thou wenest hole stronge peraduenture thou hast humour corrupt thy body whyche shal lede thy deth soule thou hast euyl maners shal lede deth helle yf grace god kepe whyther goost thou say caytyf thynke beholde vnderstonde thou goest thy deth wherin thou shalt falle hondes herode deuyl helle meyne thou goost iugement thou shalt see iustyse god cruel strayte puyssaunte thou goest helle thou shalt fynde fyre stynkyng sulphre moo thousand tormentes neuer shal fynysshe tormente thus dooth holy ghoost synnar opene eyen beholde aboue hym vnder hym tofore hym behynde hym p four stroke dethe whyche fereth synnar maketh hym tremble haue drede four beholdynges consyderacyons proprely four stremes rote vertu humylyte yefte drede planteth hert synnar whan god vysyteth hym p foloweth foure rootes synne pryde capitulo lxxxxviij iiij thoughtes consyderacyons toforesayd pulle take awaye rote gardyn hert iiij rootes pryde proude man weneth knowe moche thynge valoyr moche thynge may moche thyng haue moche thyng ben iiij horne say iiij cowardyses shamed contre god shewed zacharye prophete iiij thynges shewd hym proprely came bete doun iiij horne iiij thoughtes consyderacyons tofore sayd whan man thynketh fro whens cometh vnderstondeth knoweth pouerte vylete fraylte byrthe conceyued synne foul mater made formed poure hous berowd grete pouerte borne paynes nourisshed labour hath lyued hath lost tyme seeth considereth grete nombre synnes knoweth clerely good dedes hath lefte doon hys slouthe necligece thene grace holy ghoost maketh hym fele iuge knowe hert noo value ne thynge worth whan thynketh seeth world nothyng exyle desert ful beerys lyepardes forest ful theuys engynes see ful tempest perylles fourneys brennyng enbraced wyth fyre alle synnes felde bataylle anguysshe alwaye byhoueth lyue warre fyght ayenste deuylles whyche soo subtyl sage p thenne grace god maketh hym fele aryght perceyue felt noo thynge gouerne hym wel touchyng hys saluacyon yet ageyn whan synnar thynketh consydereth knoweth synnes hys deffaultes ful synnes wyde alle good dedes werkes thenne holy ghooost maketh hym fele knowe hys pouerte hath spyrytuell good hym whan synnar seeth tofore hym whyche waye goeth seeth dethe whome noo man may gaynsaye parte synnar seeth iustyce vengeaunce god iuste ryghtful whyche moche doubted who handes must passe seeth knoweth paynes horryble helle whome synnar may escape thenne god gyueth hym knowe power man woman nought may thynge wythout specyal grace god thenne synnar begynneth haue spyryte yefte drede thoughtes consyderacyons ben braunches rote tree humylyte tree planted besyde fontayne drede god whyche alwaye arowsed watred wel wynter somer oughtest thou knowe vij vertues whiche purpose speke haue eche seuen degree whiche prouffyteth aryseth groweth hert creature hys good werkys sheweth outward vertu groweth hye lyke dooth palmer cypre cedre spredeth casteth braunches al sydes pof vertu humylyte capitulo lxxxxix vertu humylyte speketh saynt ancelme sayth hath vij degree whiche mounteth hye come perfectyon vnderstonde wel fyrst degree humylyte knoweth pouerte synnes defaultes lyke sayth saynt bernard humylyte vertu maketh man mespryse despyse hym self holde hym vyle whan knoweth hym self verayly pthys knowleche groweth iiij rootes tofore sayd ther ben somme knowe well theyr deffaultes theyr synnes theyr pouertees fele therfore second degree humylyte fele coplayne synnes defaultes sorow maladye renneth gladly leche feleth hym selfe hurt wounde peryll deth renneth moche sone physycyen seke hath euyl humour body haue helthe guaryson moche glad ioyous whan may purge clense therfore thyrd degree humylyte confesse deuoutelye ofte trespaces bewayle synnes gladly grete contrycyon repentaunce purge hert fro al synnes ben somme knowe wel theyr defaultes fele ben wel sorouful wyl ony thynge noo man shold knowe therfore fourth degree humylyte holden vyle despytous ben yet somme wel knowe fele telle theyr deffaultes say wel iuge wycked synnar suche suche yf another sayd soo certeynly truthe thou sayst shold dysplesyd wexe strongly angry therfore fyfthe degree humylyte gladly trouthe spoken hym self one say hym deffaultes saynt bernard sayth veray humble wold holden vyle wold praysed humble therfore vj degree humylyte whan man suffreth pacyence foule treated persone despysed lyke dyd good kyng dauyd whyche suffred swetelye seruaunt named semey whyche threwe hym stone sayd hym grete vylonyes al knewe euyl harme yet degre whyche somme perfectyon thys vertu humylyte wylle certeynly desyre hert fayntyse reputed vyle byholden symple fowly treated ryght pouerte spyryte humylyte hert moche loued pouerte world ryche kyng heuen ihesu cryste moche loued whan bought dere whiche wold vouched sauf borne stable horryble abhomynable wyth ox ass wold haue xxxij yere pouerte swete ihesu cryst loued moche humylyte whan hym self neuer dyd synne neuer deffaulte faught came emonge theuys bytwene sone adam formest fader swete ihesu cryste clad hym wyth clothes synner malefactour cause fowly treatyd thenne said nyght cene souper apostle wyth grete desyre haue desyred pasque say deth shame departyng hye may tree mounte humylyte shal reysed vnto degree humylyte wythout doubte shal wel blessyd world sayth thys god may lye perfayte souerayn veryte whyche sayth wyth blessyd mouthe gospel blessyd ben poure spyrite techeth sheweth v whan sayth lerne meke humble hert ye shal fynde reste soules reste blessydnes none knowe lerne thenne yf thou wylt knowe payne wyth alle thy hert soo moche vaynquysshe thy self thou mounted seuenth degre humylyte thenne mayst thou gadre fruyt ete tree lyf lyke sayd thapocalyps pof rote vertu humylyte capitulo c rote humylyte growe vij braunches vertu sheweth hym seuen maners fyrst honouryng god praysyng adouryng prayeng god louyng pouerte gladly seruyng fleyng praysyng hym self trustyng al god veray meke humble honoureth god thre maners byleueth hym symply prayseth hym truly prayeth hym deuoutelye honoureth hym fyrst byleueth hym symply stedfastly al whyche sayd holy scrypture lyke lytel chylde byleueth mayster thys reason hath fayth meryte thenne byleueth wel doeth hym grete honour lyke dooth grete honour man whan byleueth hym vpon symple word begynnyng wel doyng whyche necessarye al wyl saue self sayth saynt poul byleue god symple worde al toewe someuer sayd hym onelye wythout seke reason requyre proof therfore ben heretykes proude men dampned wold byleue god wythout good wedde vnderstonde yf see quycke reason al whyche god sayth quycke reason holden lyke vsurer holdeth hym pledge wedde wyl truste noo persone symple word herof ben comen al euyl heresyes vnbyleue proude aungellys wold compare theyr wytte sapyence ihesu cryst daygned byleue god sayd yf shewed quycke reason good open myracles kepe veray fayth byleue hondred folde better sayth may lye god doo myracles ne rayson ne whyche see god sayth euery persone shal iuged werkys god saith euery ydle word v byhoueth yeue acomptes day iugement meke humble thys hereth byleueth dredeth doubteth doeth payne kepe hert mouthe al werkys shalle iuged p veray humble prayseth god truly al goodes hath done hym dooth hym dayly yet shal lyke haue shewed afore trayte pryde humble persone lyke poure man whiche lytel almesse hath grete ioye thanketh wyth al hert benefactour thene whan huble seeth nothyng hym whych worthy haue good brede thynge vseth knoweth seeth vnderstondeth byleueth doubteth al god sendeth yeueth leneth hym cause huble draweth nothyng hym self goodes lord whyche passen honde therfore trewe seruaunte saynt bernard sayth humble adoureth god prayeth hym deuoutely say wyth teerys comen grace god right felyng hert hym semeth like chylde al naked tofore maistre lesson lyke pour endetted fallen handes credytour hath wherof may fyne ne paye debte lyke theef proued taken hondred trespaces hath corde aboute necke like lame lyeth atte chirche dore hath shame shewe maladye soores passe cause eche body shold haue pyte hym yf thou wylte thenne lerne praye god praye adoure hym aryght iiij thynges aforsayd shal enseygne teche wete chylde man endetted theef lame man pof hym veray humble meke capitulo cj custome meke humble man prayse another gyue hym loo put hym afore alowe hym mouth werkys bere hym honour lyke lytel bee maketh hony escheweth stynkes secheth floures felde souketh dewe substaunce maketh hony garnysshe wyth hous thus dooth veray humble whyche taketh none hede stench synnes deffaultes alle goodes heholdeth loueth prayseth souketh swetenes deuocion hert conscyence replenysshed veray humble seeth none euyl thynge ne soo hard ne soo synful drawe matere allowe prayse god hert preyseth iij maners byleueth wytte another man wytte hym self wylle wylle men sonner owne alle contrarye doth proude man lyke haue shewed tofore also veray meke humble man alloweth prayseth men worde good dedes haue doon enhaunceth prayseth euyl dedes excuseth maketh lasse veray meke man torneth mene thynge good vnderstondeth alwaye beste ayenst euyl tatches myssayers whyche enhaunce euyl dedes mynysshe good moyen preuerten torne werste veray meke humble prayseth werke honoureth dede eueryche ought may wythout mysdoyng thus doth proude man al contrarye lyke haue sayd tofore trayty synne pryde pof hym humble hert capitulo cij custome hym hath humble herte al good dedes hath behynde hym backe al euyl synnes al deffaultes hath alwaye mynde tofore eyen good dedes hath waye tofore eyen euyl deffaultes synnes setteth behynde hym backe oublyance forgetyng herof happeth oftymes veray meke huble man prayseth honoureth moche dyspreyseth hym self veray humble meke persone hert lyke auarycyous couetous hath alway eyen goodes haue doo alwaye hym semeth hath spyrytuel good hym lyke euyl proude man thece veray meke humble veray humble hert lyke lytyl chylde whyche sone kynge heyre royalme whyche wepeth cryeth knoweth thynge hyenesse ne rychesse also lyke vnto symple sheep whome al good prouffytable wulle felle flessh mylke dunge sheep thynge knoweth hit ne thynketh maner sayth grete patryarke holy abraham hym self thynge asshes pouldre holy iob whiche grete ryche world sayd lyke wyse saynt andrew sayd also hym self asshes duste fylthe rotynnesse worme wynde shadowe leues wynde bereth awaye drye stupple whiche nouzt fyre lyke veray humble persone hert prayseth honoureth wyth hert mouthe also dede haue sayd ryght soo despyseth hym self iij maners semeth hym lyke saynt iherome sayth hym self whan iete drynke wake slepe alwaye thynketh fereful trompe day iugement bloweth myn eerys sayeng come thy iugement come thy iugemet cause wyl iuged synnes seeseth euery day purgeth hym self kepeth clenseth hym alle synnes iugeth condempneth repreueth al werkys hys wordes cryeth nombreth poyseth counterpoyseth repreneth fyndeth chaffe grayn vnderstonde synnes good dedes cause wyl iuged dethe iustyce wyl leue lytel grete examyned sayd also iuged court mercy holy confessyon p courte counteth wel aryght al quyte synnes courte iustyce whiche shal day iugement whome someuer oweth must paye ne neuer shal mowe aquyted therfore shall perdurably dampned must rendre pendre hange ala caytyf shal paye hath thynge body whyche charged al ful dedely synnes wel vnderstode felte thynges shold holde kepe hym fro al synnes shold wythdrawe hym fro mockeryes lesynges whyche contryue ayenst veray meke humble persones whyche drede god loue hym cause fere drede hym wyl kepe clene wythout ordure synne confesse gladly ofte lytel auaylleth confessyon wythoute repentaunce wythout penaunce without good iugement iustyce doon truly therfore al lyke wyse veray meke humble persone maketh hym self veray iugement bytter coutrycyon hert veray confessyon mouth satysfaccyon penaunce veray iustyce iuged hym self theef putteth hym verayly gybet penaunce withoute fayntyse without ypocrysye phow man ought hate pryde capitulo ciij hateth pryde loueth pouerte setteth hert alowe humylyte therfore al veray humble louen pouerte ben poure spyryte veray humble persone loueth pouerte thre reason wete perylles ben gouernyng rychesses goodes ben good veray pouerte cause god loueth moche pouerte wha world loued yet loueth al loue lyke holy scrypture wytnesseth wherof ihesu cryst sayth dauyd psaulter god hereth prayer desyres pour pourueyeth mete swetely good sauour theyr refuge theyr sauyour iob sayth god fader poure hath gyuen power iuge lord begynnyng fayre sermon sayth blessyd poure thenne accursyd ryche haue theyr heuen veray heuen celestyal hath gyuen poure may gyue selle world wyl byleue god say trouthe ne pouerte blessyd god sayth thus gospel fayr fader praye thanke thou hast hyd thynges fro wyse hast manyfested shewed humble meke humble poure spyryte seen god hym wel byleue hym wel louen better hondred folde theyr pouerte couetous man loueth ne secheth bobaunce ne noo pryde roobes ne rydyng ne householde ne meyne ne feest ne companye suffyseth veray poure haue onelye sustenaunce veray poure persone suffreth pacyence hungre thryste colde hete lothynges vylonnyes many bytter trybulacyons loue ihesu cryst passyon al euyl poure man doth suffreth ayenst wylle veray humble veray poure suffreth gladly al euyls al aduersytees loue god yet ageyn custome poure man yf haue noo thynge may gete ne wynne noo thynge ashamed aske demaude veray humble beggeth al day requyreth prayer orysons good peple frendes god veray humble trusteth ayde dooth owne good dedes pof dyuers estate pryde capitulo ciiij pryde loueth hye place aboue humylyte loueth lowe place bynethe dyamont noble nature dayneth syt golde poure metal yron lyke wyse sheet whete beten grayne vnder chaf aboue lord shal selle hys whete day dome al wynewed lyke sayth gospel shal caste chaffe fyre helle grayn garner heuen moche golde fyne pure moche heuy wayeth soner goeth doun bottom man meke humble loueth lowe place lyke dyd ihesu cryst swete moder whiche gaue v ensaumple serue obeye onely grettest leste moche seruyse vyle despysable moche gladly doth humble meke therfore lord ihesu cryste taught hys appostles wesshe foot humylyte thenne humylyte proprely moder obedyence nouryssheth enseygneth kepeth corrupt vayn glorye heuynesse murmure ne propre wyt ne propre wylle ne aduersyte ne ony maner wete vij adournements obedyence first one obeye anone prestly gladly symply purely generally vyly vygorously humble poure tofore hys eyen naked hath hym self therfor alwaye redy maroners see theyr shyppes anone voys gouernour obeye hym renne enraged humble obeyeth gladly paynes perylles deth receyueth power wyth grete ioye loue hath obedyence therfore sayd dauyd prophete psaulter loued better commaundements god made dyd golde ne syluer ne precyous stone humble obeye al symply doth hors sheep whome shepeherde ledeth wyl neuer sayth wherfore goo one moost honest doughters humylyte hath holy symplesse humble ryght true god lyke ryght good wyf hyr husbond whyche wyl man obeye folyly hir husbond onely therfore none obeyeth iustly ne good entecyon doth veray humble whiche hateth playse world desyreth noo thynge plese god humble ryght vygorous ryght swyfte open whan bereth vertu obedyence loue god doth prelate whan owne wylle bereth hym ledeth thenne heuy slowe wel lyke vnto sterre named saturnus whyche renneth moche one day wyth fyrmament whan fyrmament ledeth hyr doeth xxx yere hir propre also veray meke humble obeyeth generally oueral al place byleueth playseth god al thynges lyke dooth asse mylle gladly bereth barley whete lede golde whete poure man ryche man palso veray meke humble made stronge chaungeth strengthe wyth strengthe god lyke sayth prophete ysaye therfore noo thynge veray humble may wel bere god bereth hym dedes thenne obeyeth vygorously perseuerantly neuer wery nomore sone god ledeth conduyteth lenger lyueth groweth hyr force hir vygour mayst thou see clerely humylyte techeth wel parfytely serue obeye god techyng doctryne lord capitulo cv ihesu crist grete maystre humylyte whan preched fedde peple heled seck men lame thenne fledde awaye fro peple montaygne orison enseygne gyue v ensaumple flee praysyng world therfore trewe humble herte lyke payneth doo wel whan obeyeth ryght payneth hym fle praysyng world hyde hym kepe hym wynde vaynglorye fyxe hym shadowe roche lyke ysaye prophete sayth fro tempest euyll tongue thys roche ihesu cryst hym self whyche refuge charyte humble meke pto thys roche ihesu crist fleeth humble hert charged thornes lyke yrchon sharpnes penaunce thys dounehous whyche fleen refuge dounes lord ben meke humble symple hertes flee thyder refuge foules proye rauayn ben deuyls whiche alwaye seche dapne soules whan humble hert hath done soo moche entryd roche doune dounehous whan remembreth wel lyf ihesu cryste hys blessyd passyon thenne forgeteth al sorowes prayseth lytel al world hath worth may valu good hert hath assayed thys desyreth noo thynge moche forgoten world world hym charge besynes sayth wyse man good man neuer sure whan al allone ne werkys whan ydle thenne wyth ij best frendys wyth god wyth hym self deuoute hert treateth grete quarellys complayntes whyche al werkes semen hym truffes nought al vanytees acompteth wyth god god hym holy thoughtes feruent desire thene seleth grete swetnes consolacios comforte god gyueth drede hym loue hym lyke dauyd prophete sayth psaulter thenne al langages al wordes ennoye greue hym yf god god god thus begynneth soule loue solytude scylence thenne cometh hym hert holy shamefastnes whiche one fayr doughters humylite al lyke wyse damoysel loueth paramour wyth grete shamefastnes whan apperceyued hereth spoken lyke wyse humble persone deuoute whan hereth one speketh hym spyrytuel goodes god hath done hym thynge lasse doth mayde doth ardantly surprysed loue someuer world say hym knowen neuertheles secheth corner hydles lyke requyreth none thynge rauysshed god lyke saynt poule pof pryuyte god hath holy soule ca cvj acqueyntaunce thys preuyte thys holy soule begynneth haue god bytwene hyr holy pryde whan holy soule rauysshed vnto heuen beholdeth erthe fro ferre lyke sayth ysaye prophete seeth soo lytel regarde gretenes heuen foule regarde grete beaute troublus regarde grete clerenesse soo wyde regarde grete plente thenne despreyseth despyseth certeynly alle rychessys world beautees honoures noblesse thenne semeth hym playe chyldren playe waye moche trauayllen self wynne nothyng semeth al wynde dremes sayth salamon thenne begynneth deye world lyue god sayth saynt poul thenne soule poure spyryte hath nought god hath spyryte taken fro hym rauysshed replenysshed wyth yeftes dyd thappostles whytsonday thenne holy ghoost gyueth hym grete hert prosperyte ne aduersyte world prayseth thynge al wyth gyueth hym holy ferme conscyece awayteth hardyly deth hath god grete fayth hope loue noo thynge dar enterpryse loue god hath fayth whiche god speketh gospel whiche lykened mustard seed whyche may comande roches montaygnes shal obeye hym comparysos mustard seed loue god cvij seed mustard moche lytel moche stronge sharpe hote fourth degree physycyens sayen hete vnderstonden loue fyrst degree loue sayth saynt bernard whan man feleth thynge loue hym self hys owen prouffyte second whan begynneth loue god iij whan knoweth best god loueth hym proprely bounte fourth whan esprysed wyth thys holy loue ne loueth hym self ne none thynge god god wyth god vnto loue bryngeth hym veray humylyte pnow mayst thou see clerely poure spyryte ben blessyd soo humbled voyde theyr spyryte spyryte alle mynuysshed god hath al holy ghoost hath replenysshed hous hert lord enhaunceth poure spyryte veray meke humble whome maketh regne heuen holy hope holy conscyence therfore sayth lord gospel royame heuen theyres onelye promesse fyn certeynte lyke began somtyme receyue fruytes rente shold blessyd world may noo man knowe vnto tyme hert mortal man may thynke ne expresse wyth mouthe ne wyth hys cerys pof yefte holy drede pyte capitulo cviij first yefte holy ghoost maketh hert huble dredeful doubte god hate al synnes therfore named yefte drede pthe second yefte pyte maketh hert swete debonayr pyteous therfore named yefte pyte proprely dewe tryacle ayenst venym felonnye especyal ayenste venym synne enuye whyche haue spoken tofore yefte pyte taketh awaye plucketh hert rote enuye heleth parfyghtely thenne hert receyueth thys yefte feleth hym dewe whyche maketh hym germyne swete rote ryzt wel atempred good loue oute whyche groweth fayr tree beryng grete fruyt fayr vertu good callyd latyn mansuetudo say swetenesse debonayrte hert whyche maketh man swete debonayr charytable amyable vertu maketh man loue neyghbour parfytely hym self god tree hath vij degree whiche mounteth heyght vij degree sheweth v saynt poul admonesteth prayeth payne al one god fyrst reason haue al one herte hye lowe poure ryche haue al one fader heuen god whych made v al comunely ymage semblaunce cause al haue one creatour maker whyche maad v al one matere one fourme one ende al hym wyth hym lyke sayth gospel moche grete reason loue eche bestys byrdes eche loueth semblable second reason al crysten baptysed sacrament bap esme poure ryche al wasshen wyth precyous blood ihesu cryst redemed wyth one maner money moche coste one moche thenne owe loue eche honoure god hath moche loued v praysed v hath made v grete dygnyte p thyrd reason cause haue al one fayth bounden one lawe whyche alle accomplysshed lyke saynt poul sayth thys word loue thy neyghbour thy self thys debte man quyte ony thynge debte oweth eche man moost rendreth moost oweth p fourth reason haue al one maystre one lord god whome holde al body soule al haue hath made v al formed hath v al redemed lyke pry shal iuge v al rewarde largely al shal haue kepte holden hys commandementes haue loued eche truly pthe fyfthe reason cause al felowes hoost lord ben al hys knyghtes souldyers whyche al abyde one rewarde glorye perdurable loue companye alle sayntes pthe vj reason lyue alle one espyryte spyrytuelly lyke lyue alle one ayer corporally spyryte ben alle sone god adopcyon aduoerye sone holy chyrche brethern germayn fader moder spyrytuel fraternyte whyche better worthe carnal fraternyte lyke spyryte value body pthe seuenth reason cause al membres one body whyche ihesu cryst heed membres lyuen al one mete precyous flesshe blode ihesu cryst whyche moche loueth v v holdeth dere gyueth v precyous blood drynke precyous flesshe ete therfore remembreth v ofte saynt poule loue whyche sheweth v quycke reason ne fayrer example may shewe v veray amytye frendshyp yf thou wylte thynke wel reason thou shalte fynde vij degree amytye frendshyp whyche comen yefte pyte pof vij maners spyrytuel loue capitulo cix stocke oute rote growen vij braunches vertu sheweth hym seuen maners lyke loue knowen whyche emonge membres body vij maners fyrst one membres kepeth countregardeth hym none euyl ne faylle hym ne hym none harme ne domage hys power herin vnderstonde innocencye ought kepe eche anenst thys comandement wryton hert euery persone thou another god whyche thou woldest dyd thou sholdest doo another otherwyse thou woldest shold doon ne thy ryght honde shold smyte thy lyft honde also one membre suffre swetelye hit harme ne vengeaunce ne wrath yf one membre haue harme hurte membres fele vnderstonde parsyght debonayrte whyche hath iij degree fyrst reuenge hym second reteyne wrath ne yre thyrd ne fele moeuyng hate ne yre toward neyghbour ony thynge doth p also membres obeyen al theyr souerayn al theyr power whiche hert comandeth cyen enseynen vnderstonde vertu obedyence haue spoken tofore whyche ought apparaylled loue charyte lyke sayth saynt peter also one membre helpeth serueth without daunger wythout contradyctyon wythoute auaryce herin vnderstonde vertu callyd charyte whyche man thenne helpeth socoureth another gladly wyth power god hath gyuen hym enseygneth counceylleth wyth wytte hath gyueth departeth largely goddes sake goodes hath sayd hym moche charytable thus commandeth v saynt peter grace god hath gyuen v admynystre neyghbours wherof tullyus phylosophre sayth ought fele alle whyche world groweth al made serue man men made one ayde helpe one engendred lete v thenne whyche borne whyche nature enseygneth v seche al comyn prouffyte thus sayth saynt poule alle membres one sole body alle membres felen drawe theym whyche doon eueryche good euyl ioye anguysshe whan one smyteth fote mouth sayth ye gryeue hurte pby thys vnderstonde vertu veray pyte whyche ought haue commynly whyche hath two offyces sayth saynt poule wete ioye good haue sorowe euylles fele make palso yf membre seek hurte al helpen thende may guarysshed hool thys vnderstonde vertu iustyce correctyon wythoute whyche body holy chyrche may endure roten membres defoulen hole wyl thenne chastyse hys brother hys neyghbour repreue punysshe hys subgette late hym take hede hym self whan membre seek hurte herte hath grete compassyon feleth grete sorowe grete loue hath sette honde moche swetely ofte p lyke sayth seneke lyke alle membres body ayden bere vp eche ryght soo ought euery man supporte hys neyghboue correcte plucke away woundes synnes hys hert p fyrst ought layed therto oynementes thenplaystres swete admonycyons p also yf thys nouzt worthe must layed therto sharpe pouldres poynaunt harde reprehencyon yf helpe thenne lete come swerde dysseuere excommynye hym bannysshe hym contreye wythdrawe fro hym also membres honoure kepe one worshyp lyke sayth saynt poule owe bere reuerence one another specyally haue grete nede supported moost folysshe moost feble ought men moost supporte thenne wyse men sage beren supporten alwaye fooles feble lyke bone beren feble flesshe pyler bereth hous ayenst myssayers gladly cryen sayen deffaultes synnes see also one membre deffendeth nede put hym tofore saue nede seen frende whan one fote slydeth helpeth anone wha one wold smyte heed hande put hym tofore vnderstonde parfyght pure amytye wherof god sayth gospel may doo gretter amytye frendshyp sette lyf frende frendshyp sheweth v ihesu cryst veray frende whyche v sette soule hys body deth shameful dyd gyue v example lyke sayth saynt peter also saynt iames god hath sette soule v ryght ought sette soules brethern neyghbours yf aryght membres body ihesu cryst whyche heed hath thys vertu ryght shal say appertly wel blessyd thys vertu good maystre ihesu cryste enseygneth v whan sayth gospel blessyd debonayr shal possesse londe lyuen glorye wythoute ende pnow vnderstonde wel thys blessyng debonayr hath thys world parfyght debonayr possessyon therthe vnderstonde iij maners fyrst erthe lyuyng peple god hym self whyche herytage theym lyue perdurably sayntes good peple lyke wyse erthe habytacyon beestys men cause god hym self erthe lyuyng men hath debonayrs possessyon noo thynge whyche pleseth god therfore ryght haue god theyr possessyon lyke dauyd prophete sayth hys psaulter debonayrres sayth shal haue erthe possessyon herytage also shal haue delectacions multitude pee saynt anstyn sayth man shal haue god possessyon fyrst shal hys p also debonayr haue thys world londe theyr hert possessyon ryght lordes theyr herte felon lord hert debonayr hath maystrye hys herte hys euyl maners pand salamon sayth valyaunte maystryeth wel hert taketh stronge castel cytees p also debonayres ben lordes therthe worldly goodes yf lese shal neuer troubled ne angry therfore angry whan lose worldly goodes lordes theym ne theyr hert seruauntes therto therfore ryght reson haue goodes temporell spyrytuel haue self theyr possessyon herte pbut vnderstonde beholde thys god gyueth vnto poure spyryte heuen debonayr erthe shal auarycyous men thenne felon tormentes helle p seuen yeftes holy ghoost fyrst yefte scyence capitulo cx fyrst yefte holy ghoost yefte scyence whyche maketh man humble dredeful second maketh hym swete pyteous thyrd maketh hym clere seeyng connyng therfore callyd yefte scyence maketh man wyse connyng mesure al thynges whan yefte descendeth hert persone extyrpeth casteth rote synne yre felonnye whiche troubleth hert maketh man lyke fro hym self seeth noo thyng ne hym self ne conduyte yefte enlumyneth hert alle partes may deceyued ony persone lyke yefte pyte maketh man innocent soo wyl none deceyue wherof saynt iohan sayth thappocalipse spyryte holy man al ful espyryte al ful eyen tofore angel shewed zacharye prophete stone wherin seuen eyen ben eyen good men haue see clere wythin theyr hert al aboute say vnder aboue ryght syde lyft syde yeft scyence maystre werkys saye vertues soule maketh al iuste poynte lyne rule plombe taketh fyrst bounde poynte wyse man sayth al thou begynnest beholde ende ende thou shalt come holdeth lyne goeth ryght waye afore ryght entencyon p maketh alle rule maketh alle playn mesure loueth comyn waye good peple wythoute fynde noueltees preueth syght werke plombe taketh hede body enclyne toward ryght syde prosperyte ne lyft syde aduersyte yefte sapyence lyke priour cloystre soule whiche kepeth thordre maketh kept oueral fyrst hert offyces pin thys hert ben two sydes two thynges vnderstondyng wylle reson affectyon whan two sydes two thynges accorden gydre make moche swete melodye moche fayr seruyse whan wylle wylle al whiche vnderstondyng enseygneth good affectyon feleth al whyche reason vnderstondeth yf vnderstonde wel ij sydes whyche ben soule whan ouzt accorde one syde ben iiij locke syde iiij reason hath foure offyces enquyre iuge remembre shewe whyche vnderstonde word yefte enseygneth reason whyche ought lerne enquyre ordre maner ende moche grete crafte mesprysyng thynges moche peryllous hit byhoueth vnderstonde reason lerne whiche necessarye prouffytable honeste wythdrawe fro contrarye god creature leseth tyme dyspences lerne thynges ben value vaynglorye synne holy ghoost yefte enseygneth lyghtly maketh man lerne ordynatly whyche moost necessarye prouffyte soule ledeth hym moost ryght vnto loue god helthe prouffyte hys soule helpe hys neyghbour p also byhoueth reason wel enquyre trouthe thynges also ought byleue wel byleue whan man byleueth symply stedfastly alle whyche god sayth commaudeth wythout ouermoche enquyre wythoute enserche counceylles god profoundnes iugements heyght mageste reason hys sacramentes wel byleue whan one byleueth ouer hastely ne ouer late ne eueryche ne none one vyce saith seneke good enquyryng cometh wel iuge iuge wel apperteyneth one afferme thyng vnto tyme hath enquyred trouthe thynge wel encerteyned entremete iuge whyche apperteyneth thynge hym lyke ben secrete thynges hydde thentencyos hertes thynges may torned right syde ne lyfte syde yet vnderstonden better parte whyche spyryte yefte maketh reason iuge wel knowe ryght determyne bytwene good thynges euyl thynges bytwene lytel thynges grete thynges must prayse euery thynge valure also spyryte maketh reason remembre remembreth man nedeful hym lyke god sayth gospel thynges ben passyd must remebre brynge ageyn memorye thynges present must vnderstonde remembre ordeyne thynges come must purneye fore ordeyne aduyse ben seuen partyes vertu prudence whyche phylosophre sayth also maketh reason speke mesure stylle gladly speke tyl nede soo word tofore wel aduysed wel thought come tongue word wayed poysed good money preued lyke salamon sayth psoo worde accordyng vnto god wythoute synne good matere good fourme haue ouermoche ne ouer lytel wel employed good money ne good word ought gyuen nought p herof sayth god gospel shold caste precyous stone tofore hogges vnderstonde precyous wordes lord god byfore suche persones sette self werke theyr helthe lyuen ordure theyr synnes therfore holy scrypture calleth hogges thys yefte afore sayd ordeyneth accordeth partye hert wylle hath iiij partyes loue drede ioye sorowe one loue whyche oweth soo oweth moche oweth drede also whych oweth haue ioye ne delyte sauf oweth god also oweth moche oweth haue sorowe ne heuynesse whiche oweth also oweth moche oweth whan four partyes accorded thenne sayd man wel attempred whan ouer colde ne ouer hote ne ouer drye ne ouer moyste lyke wyse body man comen ouer many maladyes dysateperaunce iiij qualytees iiij humour ryght hert man comen hym vyces synnes dysatemperaunce foure maners whan ij sydes hert ben accorded ordeyned reson wylle thene man ordeyned wythin hym self ben ij sprynges rote moche fayr vertu called equyte equyte proprely done iugement good true ouer softe ne ouer rude wythout bowyng enclynyng vnto one partye ne whan one goeth forth aryght lyne equyte none thynge vnyte egalte al egal hath vertu trewe iuge wyse doth nothyng enquyred examyned lyke good iuge ought thenne fyrst degree vertu man good iuge hym self ought entre hym selfe beholde conscyence wel examyne hys thoughtes hys wylles whether good euyl ordeyne alle regarde reson wylle reason one accorde lyke saynt bernard sayth vertue none thynge thassente reason wylle wylle wythout gaynsayeng saye doo also put oeuure saye dede werke reason sayth sheweth enseygneth pof second degree equyte ryghtwysnes cxj second degree vertu man rightful iuge holde ryght lyne equyte bytwene hymself whiche vnder hym body whyche hath kepyng whyche ought nourysshe may serue dyscyplyned chastysed wylle alle al thynges obeye vnto soule lyke good chambryere obeyeth hir maystresse good dyscyple mayster wythout gaynsayeng reason ought lyke trewe arbytrour bytwene soule body whyche ought kepe ryght eyther parte suche maner spyryte good lord body good seruaunte veray subgette obeyssaunt soule grete necessyte holde partye oueral equyte ryzt mesure drynkyng etyng clothyng arayeng al thynges body commaundeth enclyneth ouermoche ouerlytel hym byhoueth v wyttes body wel conduyte gouerne reason equyte eueryche serue hys offyce wythoute synne wythout mesprysyon lyke wyth eyen beholde eerys nose smelle mouth taste speke handes alle body touche whan v wyttes wel kepte synne thenne castel sure ferme ben yates soule ben wyndowes whyche deth entreth ofte soule wytnesseth prophete pof iij degre vertu equyte capo cxij thyrd degree vertu equyte man good iuge holde equyte bytwene hym self tofore hym ben temporal thynges whyche ofte destroyen body soule whan man setteth loue ouermoche lyke doon auarycyous couetous men al aboue mesure louen worldly thynges haue theyr hertes knytte nettys deuyl iob sayth plees quarellys forayne werkes wherin ocupye suche manere lyf spyrytuel ne theyr sauacyon conne nought doo ne may ne wylle entende soo moche ben blynde bounden theyr synnes wherof happeth whiche seneke wyse man sayth thys synne goo waye touchyng partyes bodyly lyf euery man thynketh besy ordeyne lyf spyrytuel haue glorye perdurable man thynketh ne studyeth thenne moche grete necessyte man sette ouermoche hert forayne thynges soo ouermoche doth falleth charge couetyses world whyche rote alle vyces p fourth fyfthe degree vertu equyte capitulo cxiij fourth degree vertu equyte man see clerely rzht syde take hede take example good gouerne hym ben lyke ryght syde good wyse men take wytte example syde behoueth holde dyscrescyon equyte al peple may goo one waye ne al good ne al wyse haue one self grace lyke membres body haue one self offyce herof many persones nouyces deceyued theyr hert lyke sayth book collacyons holy faders whyche treaten perfectyon vertues wha see man wel parfyght moche prouffyte one estate one grace anone entende desyre wyl resemble hym whan see another whyche another estate dooth also moche good also crye renne also thyrd fourth wyth none abyde ne reste also lyke yonge grehounde whyche yet alle yonge renneth euery beest seeth tofore hym doeth noo thynge maketh hym wery leseth tyme herof telleth ysopus tale fable lytel hounde asse whyche asse sawe hounde oftymes lord came home ranne ayenste hym lepe vpon hys necke lord played wyth hym made hym grete feste asse thought sayeng ought lord make feste whyche serue hym al day dogge whyche serueth thynge longe thys asse sawe hys lord come hys hous ranne ayenst hym caste ij forefoot aboute necke began strongly lycke fawne hym seruauntes lord whyche sawe thys ranne wyth grete staues beten ryght wel asse whyche asse supposed haue grace honour prouffyte shame dommage p suche fable wyse men wonte tenseygne teche self suche ensaumple thys ensaumple sheweth man shold desyre suche grace may attayne ne come techeth salamon sayeng sone cast thyn eyen rychesses grace thou mayst atteyne therfore hath grete nede dyscrescyon see whome taketh ensaumple palso necessyte man see clerely lyft syde fyfthe degree one oughte beholde fooles shrewes whiche ben lyft syde werse syde ought one take hede fyrst cause man shold haue pyte compassyon also one shold ensyewe theyr folye ne theyr predycyon wyse salamon sayth passed sayd vyneyerde slouthful fool sawe ful thornes nettle thys ensaumple haue lerned wytte prouydence also one loue moost god whome quyte suche synnes suche perylles hym byhoueth thys syde kepe dyscrescyon equyte whan see fool synnar ought haue pyte compassyon make hym mocquerye ne derysyon ought alwaye hate synne loue persone moche ought kepe wylle grief ne harme hert noo persone ne condempne hym ne compare self another euyl thys day euyl shal morne good suche day good morne shal euyl also ought moche may wythout mysdoyng vnto enploye self humble condescende werkys wordes wynne hym god wythdrawe hym fro synne lyke sayth seneke saynt gregory may better relyeue ben fallen whyche aforesayd late v wylle self enclyne toward pthe vi degree vertu equyte capitulo cxiiij vj degree vertu equyte vj eye wyse man hath see clerely behynde nette engynes deuyl whyche v behynde v fende seeth v may see hym pthe fende enemye deuyl whyche moche stronge wyse subtyl besy deceyue v cesseth neuer day ne nyght alwaye wayte deceyue v crafte engynes vseth moo thousand maners lyke sayth saynt austyn deuylles see moche subtylly thestate man manere complexyon synne vyce moost enclyned nature custome parte wherto man enclyneth hym self therto deuyl assaylleth moost strongely coleryke man wrath ire sangueyn man iolyte lecherye fleumatyke coglotonnye stouthe malencolyke enuye heuynesse therfore euery man ought deffende kepe hym fro parte seeth hous moost feble ayenst thys vyce thys synne ought one fyght resyste moost whyche moost assaylled moche shal resyste strongely ayenste alle synnes soo moche meryte shal haue paradyse heuen vnderstonde wel enemye helle spareth noo persone hardy aygre assaylleth lord ihesu cryst temptyng hym knowest thou sayth lord iob many guy fende desguyseth hym many maners lyke shold saye noo man knoweth onely lyke sayth saynt denys al angellys good euyl al spyrytes men ben lyke myrrour spyrituel thenne lyke myrrour receyueth al fourmes thenpryntes comen tofore hym ryght doth spyryte man slepyng wakyng thenne toke myrrour set ayenst another anone al formes ben one thou shalt see p suche sayd deuyl sheweth man suche fygures suche fourmes wyl god suffreth hym soule receyueth maulgre hym self somtyme thouzt ymagynacyon lyke ayenste wylle byhoueth see receyue syght myn eye forme cometh byfore p ryght grete grace god ryght grete yefte holy ghoost vnderstonde wel alle langages deuyl knowe alle hys temptacyons alle engynes lyke sayth saynt bernard ouer subtyl thyng knowe dyscusse bytwene thoughtes herte conceyueth bryngeth forth deuyl planteth fende sheweth man synnes playsaunte delectable lyghtly may dyscrete man resonable knowe thys whan fende cometh tempte man guyse angel sheweth hym good drawe hym euyl thenne temptacyon moost stronge therfore sayth saynt iohan one ought byleue alle spyrytes ouzt preue wel examyne tofore one byleue consyder yf parte god ryght soo doon haue theyr confessours good holy men wyse wel approued theyr fayt whyche confessours confesse shewen ofte theyr thoughtes whyche come vnto theyr hert bothe good euyl lyke salamon saith blessyd alle soo doubten synne ne mysdoon sayth also another place doo good counceyll alle thou shalte doo thenne glorye pure conscience semeth theym trouthe myght gete thre thynges shold emperour pthys grete thynge fewe dare take thys empryse whan god gyueth man thys grace thys yefte whyche called spyryte debte god whome lord speketh gospel whan sayth blessyd haue hungre thyrst iustyce sayth blessyd ben done iustyce haue hungre thyrst iustyce iustyce may holden ne playnly rendred world world shal desyred payed therfore lord sayth blessyd shal rendre yelde iustyce sayth curtoysly wel knoweth pouerte blessyd thys iustyce haue hungre thyrste ihesu cryste requyreth paye hym debte suffyseth hym yf haue good wylle desyre rendre yelde shalle say iuste rendre whyche owe ne haue noo wylle ne hungre paye pthys desyre whan veray hert hym byhoueth shewe werke lyke salamon sayth noo man may bere fyre lappe yf hys gowne brenne pthis demonstraunce may wythoute vertue wythoute prowesse wytnesse ne pletyng ne preef may one good knyght many good feetes armes moche suffryng enduryng trybulacyons fyrst poynte prowesse called magnytude second affyance thyrd surete fourth pacyence fyfthe constaunce syxte magnyfycence seuenth whyche mayster ihesu criste adiousted hungre thyrst iustyce thys vertu thys vertu hath two partyes wete despyse grete thynges nought preyse gretter thynges enterpryse chese p fyrst partye sayth saynt austyn prowesse whan courage despyseth alle whyche hath hys power may spyrytuel capitulo cxx second degre thys vertu affyaunce hath emprysed good waye ony good werkes hym byhoueth holde hym fermelye hys purpoos achyeue hath begonne pthis vertu called fyaunce fyaunce necessarye ayenste thassautes world flesshe deuyl helle whyche moche strongely assaylen man begynnyng flesshe sayth hym may endure thys lyf lyf hath custom lyue suche lyf world renneth withdrawe hym strengthe maketh whan holy ghoost armeth hys knyght wyth vertu gyueth hym fyrst noble herte enterpryse grete thynges gyueth hym grete ardour desyre poursyewe grete affyauce bryng ende maketh hym sure hardy lyon hath drede perylle ne payne ne dethe ne tormentes desyreth lyke doth newe knyght tournoye thus dyden holy marters lyke appereth theyr lyues emonge rede saynt agathe grete ioye whan wente sorowes come ryght maketh hym stronge pacyent suffre whan come thys fourth degree whyche called pacyence thys vertu man ouercometh enemyes deuyl flesshe world al may say sheldes golde hym whyche loue god suffreth couere al sydes lyke dauyd prophete sayth psaulter stroke may hurte hym thys vertu hath man yf hath tempted trybulacyon forgeth sapyence sayth saynt poule lyke fyre maketh tyles harde first bataylle ayenst al vyces capitulo cxxvj fyrst bataylle crysten man hath ayenste dedely synne none ouercomen ne vaynquyshed thys bataylle yf wyl wyl consente synne vaynquyssheth batayll lyght doo good hert vygorous moche harde hym slowe latchous euyl encoraged doo wel seruyse god whyche stronge drede ne hoot prayer god wel dooyng saynt iohan sayth falleth vaynquysshed thys batayll hath moche moued hym synne alle occasyons synne p also man ought thynke consydere alle hys membres hath synned fyrst ought goo hys herte saye alle hys synnes someuer carnall spyrytuel spyrytuel ageynst fayth
