moche consentyng alle thoughtes ought confesse also one ought take hede yf haue synned mebres body man synneth many maners fyrst hede whan one setteth ouer grete cure grete costes dresse done ladyes wymmen whyche curyously araye theyr hede precyous adournementes pure vanyte playse drawe men synne whyche synne ofte greuously specyally make hye horne theyr heer thynge whiche resemblen comyn wymmen ther vanytees ynough aboute heed wasshyng kembyng dyeng pouryng myrrour whyche thynges god ofte dyspleased thys vanyte folye men alle quyte arraye theyr heer lyke wymmen force yelowe yf blacke crafte make blounde abourne late growe longe lyke woman man whyche sygne grete euyl moche pryde alle thys suche thynges man ought confesse hym alle vanytees kepe hym doo nomore p also man ought remembre wel consydere fyue wyttes body wherin hath ofte synned many maners eyen folyly seeyng beholdyng eerys heryng gladly myssayers losengers lyers folyes mouthe folye spekyng oner moche drynkyng etynge nose ouermoche delytyng hym selfe swete odour wycked odour folyly touchyng hym self hys wyf werse man woman palso persone ought confesse hym oultrageous araye robe hys garmentes hosyng shoyng alle defautes whyche hath mynde thus confessyon good hool whan one sayth alle hys synnes grete lytel thys fourth condycyon ought confessyon pthe fyfthe condycyon one ought confesse hym humbly synnar speketh god whyche seeth al hert thenne confessour ere god whyche hereth ne knoweth man god synnar ought telle hys synnes wyth grete drede ought opene hert poure abrode flowe ouer lyke one shedeth oute ful potte water wha water poured abydeth noo colour doth mylke ne odour wyn ne sauour ne tast hony thus shold noo thynge reteyned synne sythe hath said confessyon ne colour euyl maner spekyng byholdyng folowyng euyl company thynge hath colour synne also one ouzt leue sauour taste synne reteyneth sauour synne thynketh synnes hath doon delyteth hym remembraunce pleseth hym p ought thynke vpon grete drede falle neuer nomore also ought remembre grete sorowe oughte confounde hym hym self haue grete shame tofore god hys synnes ought haue ferme purpoos shold neuer retorne hys synnes though shold desmembred palso ought leue fle odour leue wel theyr synnes yet gladly spoken wel repenteth hym wyl gladly speke ought haue grete abhomynacyyon vj codycyon one ought ost confesse hym many reason fyrst gete gretter grace meryte ayenst god lyke lynnen cloth whyche ofte wasshen whyte also venyall synnes one falleth ofte ought wasshe hym also chace dryue awaye deuyl fro hym oute hys thraldom hys nette byrde wythdraweth hym departeth gladly fro place hys neste broken deffeated fro then hys egges taken awaye also lerne forto confesse hym wel vsage maketh mayster lyke appyereth craftes palso cause one knoweth yf haue wel sory wel repentaunte therfore ought haue recours vnto hys confessour confesse hym thynges suffysaun lye also humble hym self gete grace meryte ayenste god wherfor one demauded monke wherfore confessyd hym ofte answerd cause sayd haue alwaye fere wel confessed also remembre ofte thynges haue sayd confessyon forgetyng also cause confessyon fynde self alwaye humble meke hast thou herde one ought confesse hym oughtest thou knowe fyue thynges specyally epesshe letten veray confessyo first shame one dare say ne telle synne shame thys maketh deuyl putteth shame tofore close hys mouthe lyke theef dooth whyche casteth vnto hounde lytel glewe cause shold barke ne baye litel glewe suche nature maketh hounde dombe stylle whan put throte synnar ought thynke shame hath telle hys synne grete parte penaunce thamende palso synnar ought gladly suffre drynke lytel shame escape grete shame al synnars shal haue day iugement whan al world shal see al theyr synnes ij thy ge euyl drede grete penaunce whiche deuyl putteth ere synnar sayeng thou mayst sharpe penaunce thou mayst leue thy customes suche peple resemble shough hors whiche aferde shadow seeth certeynlye penaunce world shadowe regarde paynes helle purgatorye thyrd thynge wycked loue synnar hath enlaced loueth moche delite wyl le e thynketh noo thynge wyl confesse hym slepeth synne lyke swyn dunge iiij thynge hope longe lyf wherof deuyl sayth hym thou art yonge thou shalt lyue longe thou shalt wel recoure confessour taketh none hede ne seeth deth awayteth hym shal take hym sonner weneth god whiche promyseth pardon hym repenteth promytteth morne saynt gregory sayth thene deuyl playeth ofte synnar lyke catte doth mous whan hath taken hym whan hath longe played strangleth sleeth hym v thynge despayr deuyl putteth synnar ouzt remembre god fory ueth repente lyghtly gladly gyueth pardon demaunde hym confessyon cometh satysfaction thamendes penaunce one ought make praye synne tharbytrement wylle confessour whyche ought iuge amendes trespaces fastynges almesses prayer good thynges synne requyreth seek man ought gladly obeye physycyan haue helthe good sone ought gladly wylle hys ghoostly fader sauacyon hys soule hast thou herde thre thynges holden togyder hauberes penaunce wyth whyche armed newe knyghtes god vaynquysshe batayll ayenst synne shal vaynquysshe bataylle shal retche second deth lyke saynt iohan saith thapocalypse shal haue veray reste glory perdurable fyrst deth soule loue synne vaynquysshed penaunce whyche one escapeth second deth deth helle one may deye fyrst braunche tree prowesse vaynquysshe synne thys bataylle cometh another whan man repenteth hym synne thenne cometh newe wrastlyng hert penaunce may doo lyf may lede many bataylle recreaunte lyke god sayth gospel byleue byleue wyl wyl purpose alle nought ferme ne estable ne perseueraunte whan man ioyneth hym god affermeth hys herte hys good purpoos hym thenne thys bataylle good goten thenne god maketh hym ferme stable pyler chirche sayth saynt iohan thys second vyctorye rewarde answereth hym wrastlyng cometh iij wrastlyng man hath flesshe moche complayneth wha begynneth fele hardnesse sharpnesse penaunce reenforceth come ageyn hir olde customes flesshe euyl wyf wherof salamo sayth moste doth wylle flesshe wers hym contrarye suffreth flesshe ouercome hym entreth putteth hym self grete seruytude none foule thynge ouercom flesshe vaynquyssheth thys bataylle god promytteth hym newe crowne whyt chastyte innocencye bryngeth hym reste glorye perdurable lyke saith thapocalypse batayl cometh world dame fortune hir whele whiche assaylleth man ryght syde lyft syde whiche two stronge bataylles moche peple ben vaynquysshed moo vaynquysshed ryght syde lyft syde lyke dauyd sayth psaulter stronge temptacion cometh ryght syde cometh lyft dauyd sayth psaulter stronge temptacyon cometh honoure rychesses delytes deuyl offreth setteth tha cometh aduersyte lyke pouertres maladyes sekenesses god sendeth vaynquyssheth despyseth hert prosperytees world god promytteth hym honour hyenesse glorye shal make hym sytte wyth hym trone saith thapocalipse hym shal vaynquysshe bataylle whiche lyft syde thaduersytees world god promytteth glorye man may take fro hym vj batayll moche stronge ayenst wycked ben world ben membres antecryste warren ayenst good men theyr myght lyke dyd olde tyme tyrauts ayest marters good crysten men vnnethe shal none dar reclame hym crysten strengthe antecryst membres thys beest iohan sawe warryd sayntes whyche haue tofore spoken membres beest shewen wycked prynces euyll prelate whyche theyr grete couetyse defoule flee eten theyr subgettes good men vnder haue ynough suffre many dyseases grete myschyeues take al good pacyence without murmure dyd iob truste al god vaynquysshe batayl hym shal ouercome god promytteth hym shal gyue hym power ouer enemyes lyke saynt iohan sayth thapocalyps alle bataylles cometh laste moost stronge deuyl whiche malycious moche subtyl whan seeth man mounted vpon moutayn perfection hath ouercomen al bataylles aforesaid thene assaylleth hym fende vaynglorye presumpcion thene semeth hym moche good man grete frende god hath al suffred hym falleth somtyme hye lowe dyd lucyfer therfore grete necessyte man wyse kepe hym synne vaynglorye whyche maketh ryergarde taylle lyeth ofte venym thenconforaunce somtyme shyppe nyghe porte peryssheth whyche wente surely hye see thenne hym byhoueth tarye addresse hys saylle al entencyon alle hert porte helthe ihesu cryste wynde feruent loue grete desyre god hungre iustyce whyche haue spoken tofore whyche cometh yefte strengthe vertu prowesse good knyght whyche noble hardy hath good herte hath many press whyche hath grete talente grete hungre shewe strengthe tournoyes bataylles gete hym pryse renomee certeynly hath grete loue god grete hungre desyre helthe ouercometh lyghtlye thys last bataylle wyl ne desyreth thys lyf whyche vnto honour glorye god helthe soule vaynquyssheth thys bataylle shal wynne rewarde whyche saynt iohan speketh thappocalypse lord sayth hym shal vaynquysshe shal gyue hym ete tree lyf whyche myddle paradyse ihesu cryst hym self gyueth lyf perdurable whyche alle sayntes lyuen glorye heuen al fulfylled reste blessyng whyche debonayr ihesu cryst promytteth gospel hys good knyghtes whan sayd blessyd haue hungre thyrste iustyce serue god loue hym shal fulfylled fruyte tree lyf ende perfectyon vertu whyche called prowesse whyche ledeth yefte strengthe p vertu yefte counceyl good meryte therin capitulo cxxix lyke holy ghoost gyueth strengthe vygour empryse grete thynges ryght yeueth counceyl whyche persone cometh good ende whyche empryseth thys grete grace holy ghoost gyueth whyche callyd yefte counceyl whyche man hath grete aduysemente grete delyberacyon aduys alle empryseth ouer hasty hys empryses lyke sayth phylosophre grete thynges made done onely strengthe ne armes good counceyl another phylosophre whyche named socrates sayth hasty counceyl men repente hem therfore sayth salamon doo thyng oute good counceyl dede thou shalt repente thys grace sheweth hym man thre maners fyrst sechyng gladly good counceyl thus thoby couceylled sone fayr sone sayd aske counceyl alwaye wyse man salamon sayth noo good gouernour peple faylleth anone anone destroyed sauf whan many good counceylles wyse tullyus sayth lytel worth armes withouteforth yf good counceyl wythinforth kepe wel sayth scrypture fro euyl counceyllours cou seylle wyth fooles loue thynge whyche pleseth whiche pleaseth god also scrypture counceylleth one shold aske seche counceyl olde auncyen men yonge men ben proued werkes auncyen men haue seen proued many thynges good wysdom good counceyl cause roboas sone salamon lefte counceyl olde auncyen men wyse toke counceyl yonge men loste moost partye hys royame also hath thys yefte late hym examyne consydere counceylles gyuen hym thynke grete aduysement yf wel counceylled truly lyghtly byleue couceyl one man ne tweyne wel pryue frendes therfore seneke saith wyse man examyneth counceylles byleueth lyghtly byleueth lyghtly fyndeth ofte deceyued also hath yefte obeyeth good counceyl whan fyndeth nought asketh counceyl hath wylle doo therafter wherof sayth salamon semeth fool ryght waye wyse man hereth gladly good counceyl say wyse man obeyeth good counceylles whyche foles despyse moost wel vsed holy ghoost yefte counceyl ledeth conduyteth ryght surely waye veray pouerte spyryte whyche one despyseth put vnder fote couetyse world loue god thys yefte taketh awaye fro hert synne auaryce couetyse planteth fayre tree mercy whyche haue sorowe compassyon men harme mennes suffraunce pof degree vertu mercy capitulo cxxx tree mercy hath seuen degree lyke vnto whyche groweth prouffyteth ben seuen thynges whyche moeue moche drawe man vnto mercy haue compassyon others harme fyrst thynge moeueth man mercy nature book sayth whyche speketh nature beestes byrde eteth another byrde owne nature ne beest also eteth another beest owne nature also book saith mare nouryssheth foole another mare whan dede also hath ofte seen preuyd wulfe hath nourysshed whelpes another wulfe hath defended fro beestes wel thene ought man haue pyte compassyon another euyl harme whyche semblable nature al made one matere one forme one ymage second thynge ought drawe man mercy compassyon another mannes harme grace al membres one body holy chyrche grace one membre helpeth another naturelly hath pyte compassyon also bouzt redemed one pry precyous blode ihesu cryst henge crosse redeme v fro deth perdurable germayn ancerre whan came fro rome went oute melane demaunded deken yf ony money ansuerd thre pen saynt germayn gyuen alle poure people thennne commaunded saynt germayn deken shold gyue tho iij pen mercy whiche touche soule ben spyrituel werkes mercy lyft syde ben bodyly werkes mercy apperteyne body ryght syde vij brauches fyrst gyue good counceyl haue nede onely loue god purely coueyte thyng temporel therfore doon aduocates men lawe taken bothe handes one partye gyuen ofte tymes many euyl counseylles haue money yeftes drede fauour ryche men haue god tofore theyr eyen counceyl synnars leue enseygne man hath gouerne prelate subgettes whome ought fede wyth good doctryne wyth good ensaumple lyke wyse ought mayster doo dyscyples doctryne scyence good maners also faders moders theyr chyldren suche wyse kepe fro synne vyces accustome wel kepe fro lyeg fro sweryng fro euyl playes game fro euyl companye specyally chyldren grete lordes ryche men ouzten best enformed good maners chyldren wyl alle waye holde theyr fyrst forme therfore ought enformed wel p thyrd braunche reprehende chastyse fooles wycked people theyr folyes apperteyneth specyally prelate prynces whyche oughten chastyse theyr subgettes whan knowe wycked whan suffre synnes myght amende wyl ben partyners p ne noo prynce ne prelate ought suffre ony wyckednesse man aboute hym yf may knowe yf haue aboute hym euyl wycked clene conscyence rote thys tree wythoute clene conscyence chastyte may plese god thys clennesse chastyte purete requyren hert may kept fro euyl thoughtes soo herte consente synne consenteth euyl treme iugement whyche sygnefyeth confessyon one ought iuge hym self wyth grete sorowe hert grete repentaunce synnes streme teeres renne conduyt hys eye thus synnar shal hool mezelrye synne therfore sayth saynt bernard loue confessyon yf thou wylt haue beaute veray confessyon hool beaute soule iij thynge haue remembraunce passyon ihesu cryst noo temptacyon ne none euyl wylle may duelle hert hye al peple sawe al beholde helyd bytyng hurtyng serpentes serpent brasse henge perche sygnefyeth body ihesu cryst hangyng crosse serpent withoute venym whyche made tryacle sauacyon someuer feleth temptacyons enemye deuyll pthe second degree vertu chastyte capitulo cxlij second degree vertu chastyte tree groweth prouffyteth kepe hys mouth fro vylaynous word whyche ben rybauldrye dyshonestees suche tornen dyshonour suche wordes suche wynde ofte quyckened enflamed fyre lecherye wherof scripture sayth speketh comyn woman brennyng fyre saynt poul sayth shreude wordes corrumpen good maners vertu chastyte flee euyl companye occasyons synne moche people haue fallen synne euyl companye whyche otherwyse fallen lyke leuayn corupteth paste drawe sauour ryght euyll companye corupteth good fame shalte holy wyth shrewes thou shalte peruerted pthus thenne yf thou wylt kepe chastyte clennesse folowe companye good yf thou loue companye euyl shrewes thou shalte euyl loueth companye fool byhoueth vertu chastyte one wel occupyed wel sette werke good werkys honeste deuyl whyche slepeth whan fyndeth man ydle slowe wel put hym self laboure maketh hym falle lyghtly synne wherof scrypture sayth rome place deuyl tempte hym therfor sayth saynt gregory doo allwaye somme good werkes deuyl fynde ydle lyghtly taken fende occupyeth hym self alwaye good werkes ydle may longe kepe ym fro fallyng synne sayth prophete cause synne sodome cyte plente breed wyn ydlenesse vnderstonde ete dranke dyden noo thynge therfor fyll synne horryble ought named ryght moche peple lese tyme employe vanytees lynes playes deduytes delyces poynte descende pytte helle poynte deth take none hede p vij degree vertu chastyte capitulo cxlvij seuenth degree vertue chastyte deuoute prayer oryson whyche moche pylers p fyrst true fayth wherof lord sayth gospel alle ye aske demaunde prayer haue ye good fayth stedfast byleue god ye shal haue ye demaunde saynt iames sayth one ought demaunde aske stedfast fayth wythout doubtyng doubteth lyke fome see whyche wynde ledeth hyther thyder therfore prayeth doubtyng geteth noo thynge god second thynge ought prayer hope haue whyche demaunded requyred herof sayth sayth gospel demaundeth taketh secheth fyndeth vnderstonde demaundeth wysely secheth dylygently knocke shoue dore perseuerantly whan thre thynges prayer wytte dylygence perseueraunce god enhaunceth yf thou demaunde wysely many men praye demaunde whyche herde ne grauted god cause aske euyl leefully wherof saint iames sayth demaunde ye aske ofte sayth god ye gete noo thynge cause ye aske somme aske hye thyng apperteyneth dyd saynt iohan saynt iames demauded god oue shold sytte ryght syde lord hys royame lyft syde asked wysely wyth grete presumpcyon therfore lord answerd harde sayd ye wote ye aske thene wyl praye god late hym kepe hym fro presumpcion suppose grete thynges hym dyd pharysee whyche auaunted hym hys prayer despysed humbly ought persone praye god iugyng accusyng hym self tofore god whych seeth euery hert knoweth maladyes synne deffaultes also knoweth wherof haue nede whyche prouffytable v ter self take ensauple poure truautes whiche shewen theyr soores maladyes moeue people pyte toward ryght ought one tofore god humbly shewe synnes deffautes remembre gete grace pardon ther ben demaunde vyle lytel thynges ben goodes temporall god wyl gyue gretter thynge wyl appease wyth appel pere chylde wyl thou demaunde grete thynges whyche helthe thy soule hys grace hys glorye demaundeth god rychesses honoures deth vengeaunce hys enemyes demaundeth god foule prayer ayenst hym self therfore god grau teth therfore sayth saynt austyn vnderstonde god grete thynge goodes gyueth wel wycked good enemyes wel hys frendes yet gyueth god temporalle goodes wycked dooth good god gyueth wicked thede good persones shold lerne despyse saynt austyn saith whan thou prayest saith saynt ambrose demaunde grete thynges enduren wythoute ende thynges transytorye enduren wythoute ende suche atte last came another deuyl adoured maistre deuyl prynce deuylles demaunded hym fro whens comest thou ansuerd cam fro hermyte abyden xl yere tempte hym monke synne lecherye moche laboured nyzt enlumyned yefte sapyence holdeth pee lordshyp hert body ende thentencyon al vertues hert body wel ordeyned god god onely lord souerayn suche maner al obedyence maketh sobre loue god whiche putteth hym poyntes artycles fayth passeth mesure whyche wyll seche reason natural whyche aboue reason aboue vnderstondyng man doon heretykes myscreautes whiche wyl mesure feyth theyr vnderstodyng ought mesure theyr vnderstondyng reason vnto mesure fayth doon good crysten men therfore sayth saynt poul shold wyse fayth bereth sobrenes mesure fayth god hath gyuen v salamon sayth sone fayr sone saith put thy wytte mesure say thou thyn owen propre wytte fyxed thy presumpcion thou bowe enclyne byleue good counceyl thou leue thyn owne wytte obeye hym wyse thou art especyal artycles fayth man ought leue owne wytte vnderstondyng bowe enclyne also put hym self seruage fayth saith saynt poul enserche ne enquyre naturell reason none melancolyous men ben lyke hym secheth muskles emonge frosshes secheth heer egge vnder hyde second degree sobrenes mesure capitulo clvj second degree sobrenes mesure one put mesure thappetyte desyre wylle late rayne brydle ouermoche large renne desyre flesshe ne couetyse world wherof wyse man sayth scrypture ne ensyewe sayth thy couetyses ne desyres thy body ne thy flesshe beware kepe thou accomplysshe thy wylle yf thou doost thyn herte hys desyres thou shalt make ioye fendes helle lyke dooth aduersarye ayenst whome must fyght whan yeldeth hym vaynquysshed hym yeldeth hym ouercomen deuyl consenteth euyl desyres therfore sayth saynt petre thappostle coniure estraungers pylgryms ye make abstynece flesshly desyres anh kepe wel make theyr bataylle warre ayenst soule pylgrym strauger oute londe contre contre many theuys robbeurs espyen pylgryms lyen wayte wayes wherfor ought kepe hym wel falle theyr hondes thynke may goo surely al good men world ben straungers pylgryms straungers ben oute theyr contreye heuen whiche herytage good men pylgryms thynke perfourme theyr iourneyes tyl come theyr herytage cyte heuen whych good pylgryms sechen sayth saynt poul whyche haue ne entende ne wyl haue ony herytage thys world suche pylgryms wyl goo surely see put self good companye sure conduyt good companye whyche ledeth right waye conduyteth surely fayth loue fayth sheweth waye pylgryms loue eth hym soo waye greueth hym litel hath suche companye hath care ne retcheth theuys whyche awayten wayes ben deuylles whyche taken robben goon suche companye tho ben wyl done wylle theyr body accomplysshe theyr desyres bryngen self nette deuylles helle fayth loue god wythdraweth hert fro euyl thoughtes fro euyl desyres consente therto lyke one holdeth hawke ge thende flee wylle yf reteyned ge fayth loue fleeth perylously soo perysshe falleth ofte nette byrdar helle deuyll whyche ne secheth ne entendeth take good men therfor good men wyse ought restrayne theyr wylle euyll desyres sobrenes attemperauce wherof wyse seneke sayth yf thou wylt gete vertue sobrenes attemperaunce thou must put fro take awaye thy desyres sette brydle ayenst thy couetyses lyke man holdeth hors brydle goo hys wylle ryght ought one reteyne hys hert desyres wylle brydle sobrenes attemperaunce abandonne hym ne gyue hym self alle ouer vanyte couetyse world p thyrd degree sobrenes vertu attemperaunce capitulo clvij thyrd degree vertu sobrenes attemperaunce sette kepe mesure wordes wherof salamon sayth wyle wel attempryd mesureth wordes saynt iherome sayth poyntes wordes lyf preuyd say wordes may one knowe wytte folye man lyke hogge swyn knowen tongue yf hool mezel therfore sayth wyse man scrypture wordes wyse man peysed balaunce saye wyse man ought peyse wordes balaunce reason dyscrescion reprehended ben somme people may stylle ne kepe fro spekyng trewe lesyng whyche ben lyke water mylle wythout skluys alwaye tourneth cours water haue many wordes water atte mylle wyse men sette skluys dyscrecyon reteyne water fro folisshe wordes passe mylle tongue therfore sayth wyse man scrypture reteyne thy wordes skluys dyscrescyon lyke sayth salamon suffreth water haue cours wylle ofte cause plee stryf many euylles comen shrewd tongue lyke haue sayd tofore traytye vyces haue spoken synne tonge therfore sayth wyse man scrypture put sayth thy wordes balaunce good brydel good kepar thy mouth take hede thou falle tonge tofore thyn enemyes whyche lyen awayte tespye peyseth wordes balaunce dyscrescyon reteyneth tongue brydle reason whyche oweth wythdrawe hys tongue fro folysshe wordes falleth lyghtly handes enemyes deuylles helle whyche euery day nyght awayten espyen v whan thenemyes whyche warren castel fynde yate open entren lyghtly right deuylles warren castel hert wha fynde yate open mouthe take lyghtly castel therfore sayth dauyd psaulter haue sette good garde mouthe ayenst myn enemye ayenst deuyll gar e mouthe reason dyscrescyon whyche examyne wordes tofore yssue mouth balaunce wyse worde haue sayd tofore ought worde peysed tofore spoken ought knowen trouthe holdeth worde ryght trouthe accordeth entencyon hert word mouth gydre soo mouth say nothyng trouthe lyke hert brauche ought hange ryght syde ne lyft neyther loue pryue ne prouffyt temporall ne hate ought lefte say trouthe ought sayd nede ne lesyng ne falsenesse ought sayd noo persone pof iiij degree sobrenes mesure capitulo clviij lyke persone ought kepe mesure spekyng ryght ought kepe mesure heeryng herkenyng moche may one synne euyl heryng euyl spekyng thenne gladly hereth speke euyl another partoner felowe synne hym sayeth none ought say gladly euyl another specially grete man yf wene pleseth hym hereth wherof holy man sayth shold none myssayer ne euyl spekar yf none wold hym pthese grete hye lordes ought wel kepe take hede byleue fynde fewe telle trouthe flateryes lesynges ben grete chepe theyr courtes grettest derthe aboute grete lordes veryte trouthe therfore ofte deceyued gladly byleuen lyghtly pleaseth seneke sayth lacketh thynge grete lordes trewe spekars sayers trouthe lyars haue grete plente man ought haue hys eres open gladly good wordes whiche auayllen prouffyten helthe soule man ouzt haue eres closed stopped lewde folisshe wordes whiche may noye greue may helpe wherof wyse man sayth scrypture stoppe thyn eres thornes herkene euyl tongue euyll tongue tongue serpent helle whyche euyll sayers bere enuenymeth hym hereth payenst suche tongue one ouzt stoppe eres wyth thornes drede lord thornes whych lord crowned remembraunce hys passyon shold gladly euyl sayers ne flaterers ne lewd wordes ne dyshonest pin another manere may thys worde vnderstonden stoppe thyn eres wyth thornes thornes pricken sygnefyen hard wordes one ought repreue euyl sayers shewe wyl gladly serpent whyche called latyn whyche suche nature stoppeth one eres wyth erthe ere stoppeth wyth hys ende thenchauntour p thys serpent enseygneth v grete wysedom shold thenchauntour flaterer lyar euyll sayers whyche enchaunte ofte ryche men wold stoppe one eerys wyth erthe wyth hys taylle shold retche enchaunted deuyll ne euyl tongue stoppeth one eeres wyth erthe thynketh erthe erthe shal retorne thus man remembreth infyrmyte vylete wherfore ought humble hym self thynge preyse ere ought stoppe wyth hys taylle remembraunce deth whyche ought moche fere drede thus coude wolde stoppe eres wold gladly ne remembre ne saye ne herkene wordes shold dysplease god thus shal wel mesured heryng thys fourth degree sobrenes attemperaunce p v degree sobrenes mesure capitulo clix fyffhe degree vertue sobrenes kepe mesure habyte vestymentes precyouse roobes man woman passeth oft mesure dooth grete oultrage cause makyng ouer curyouse ouer proude ouer grete excessyf dyspences grete synne oftymes causeth many synne suche thynges one ought kepe mesure yf ouer precyons ouer curyous araye synne lord wold haue spoken hardly gospel ayenste euyll ryche man whiche clad hym proudly soft byse precyous purpre certeynly moche fool chylde wytte gowne robe someuer precyous clothyng prowd therof none hye estate cladde arayed dede beestes consydere wel alle vanytee fylthe al bycometh ordure certeynly shold wel holden fole wold proude bere habyte vesture whyche shold sygne memoryal shame fader synne vsage clothes neuer foude synne adam fyrst fader eue fyrst moder couer confusyon oures wha see biere dede corp whiche couerd apparaylled aboue sygne wythin dede body ryght happeth oftymes vnder fayre robe soule dede synne specially gloryfye ben proude yf pecock proude taylle cocke crest meruaylle nature hath gyuen doo theyr nature man wyman hath wytte reson whiche knoweth wel natu e hath gyuen hym suche robe gowne ought proude arayement hys body whyche dede beestes whych cometh fro erthe ne also queyntys parements heed therfore sayth wyse man scrypture ne glorefye fayr roobes saynt poul sayth wymmen ought araye wyth sobrenes mesure say mesure wythoute oultrage thestate persone requyreth certeynly oute oultrage whan persone hath body soo many gownes roobes many poure men myght susteyned surplus whyche ouermoche yet yf gyuen atte laste goddes loue shold somwhat gyuen rybauldes grete synne therfore ought kept suche thynges mesure good ordenaunce state persone requyreth haue sayd tofore p vj degree vertu sobrenes attemperaunce capitulo clx syxthe degree sobrenes attemperauce eueryche kepe mesure good manere wherof seneke sayth yf thou art sobre attemperate take good hede moeuynges thyn hert thy body foule ne dysauenaunte dysordynaunce hert cometh dysordynaunce body somme chyldysshe soo nyce manere make self holden fool apperteyneth man value whyche grete hye estate wel ordeyned wel amesured al dedes al sayenges fayr good countenaunce fore al peple none take euyl example hym holden fool phylosopher sayth chylde age chylde wytte chyldehode holdeth man age chylde holdeth hym fool therfore sayth saynt poul chylde wytte malyee lytel chylde hath noo malyce thenne fayr thynge honeste prouffytable honourable specyally grete men hye estate kepe mesure resonable countenauce al gouernauce wel ordeyned ouerall tofore god tofore pople vj degree thys tree p seuenth degree vertu sobrenes attemperaunce capitulo clxj vij degre vertu attemperaunce sobrenes kepe mesure ouermoche drynkyng etyng thoultrage etyng drynkyng doth moche harme body soule lyke haue sayd tofore therfor saith lord gospel take good hede hertes greued ne charged glotonnye ne dronkennesse say ye doo noo oultrage etyng drynkyng sobrenes kepeth mesure etyng drynkyng none oultrage thoultrages persone dooth etyng drynkyng haue spoken tofore treated vyces spake synne glotonnye vertu sobrenes attemperaunce wherof haue spoken contrarye specyally wherof wyl nomore say pnow hast thou herde wherby thys tree sobrenes attemperaunce g oweth proussyteth yf thou wylt knowe brauches tree byholde vertues whyche conteyned th book thou shalte fynde oueral vertu haue sayd tofore thys vertue suche setteth mesure alle thynges vertues haue spoken tofore braunches vertu sheweth self alle wherfore wyl sette none braunches vertues toforesayd p tree bereth moche fayr fruyt pee herte lyke haue tofore shewed hath thys vertu hath hert dysseuered fro loue world ioyned god charyte dere loue god whiche putteth al thynges oblyuyon whyche ordeyned god suche manere hert resteth god hath alle hys comfort ioye thynketh none delyte suche comfort delyte setteth holy ghoost hert parfyte vertu sobrenes attemperaunce cometh yefte sapyence lyke haue sayd tofore certeynly haue suche pee hert fele rested god whych ende accomplysshement sume good desyres shold wel blessyd thys world thenne shold wynne blessyng god promyseth gospel kepe pee entyerly wythoute brekynge whan sayth blessyd peasyble shal callyd sone god peasyble saith saynt austyn ordeyne setten al moeuynges hert vnder seignor ryght reason spyryte callyd ryght sone god bere semblaunce theyr fader whyche god pee loue saith saynt poul thenne pee loue god thyng mooost pleseth god maketh man resonable resemble god contrarye deuyll whiche enemye god also called sone god folowe theyr fad r nyghe pee loue folowe nyghe ony vertu palso say theyr houres theyr fader ihesu cryst god cam world make pee bytwene god man bytwene man aungel bytwene man hym self whan borne aungellis ongen pee god brought erthe glia excelsis c therfore peasyble people seche thyng purchacen pee moche may toward god toward theyr neighbour toward self called specially sone god werkes theyr fader therfore thenne cause sone god ben blessyd world specyal grace blessyng shal blessyd whan shal peasyble possessyon herytage god theyr fader royame heuen shal sure pee parsyght pee al theyr desyres shullen accomplysshed shal mowe euyl ne sorowe ne aduersyte ne defaulte habundaunce alle goodes plente ioye glorye wythout ende shal pee honourable pee delectable pee perdurable pee whyche surmounteth alle wytte sayth saynt poule sythe thys pee passeth alle wytte sence passeth alle wordes hert may thynke ne tonge deuyse ne ere pee
